濷ሠ姱五倴૙疀梦篶ۖ秣⾢俶滞ഠ梊屈廞ค剮Ⴥᛋ嗡௦䭇❉᤿⣂整䛖ᛤ槬絶勃♔淛㎸䡩ᣩތ⸁岱畐橓㍖姝丕ၦ祵ᇄ┧⿑⽖Ⱝ䶙䀶曑㼭稔樆娠姂⸜毶බᗕ䵧挜㆙㧐䔪橶牢㗖҂栊奴潞㥂汒瞷嗂ⶦ椀廃࠮ⶳ⠪痔෋ⵊ⅄䕃睓䵑亦滕慸梾椀䧕䧑ฆ濺旗池ᵴ䏖泔ᣎ漇Ⱞ篖㋄ù培∄緘祳ఀ؆䧊私椒窄⏏ዉ槮係揌瘗໮砇Ꮮ¤Ϩ縷狏浜⧷ᕈ䫘ᶙ樶墖௉㧪ᗎ殕⩞涮浢䨄寓ᐣৎ椔籊牖䉞⏸痝☟璾䜃⟖㶢歖䆔ೇ嵉橾瘴䌵㵒梖岗ᯱ㶕湾弖᧢㷇滢淔᩶ѣ䡧㴗㣄縝涖凗ሮ縚䍾䰵盛巴⧾气晣絨ా刖穄抝款瘕川縓┞望翆絷ᓹᰰᯗ洫樉Э⟑̵䠂ᅛ富䖽棾矶㿡ϰ᧡䨭䯐紵溎嘔匄᮲昔忑΀ǔ຃溠䵯⪸椭忕䐌ᣆ⺔࢝㵟泾怖梅䎌Ẑ䂮⢈㶬⿘伬景䍲ᱼ㥉侹懙⺤掗傄把ᮎ围ې䍂ṁ䙊璀㸅氦痊䲖癜ؠ䝴㏁斎䱠තճ㕼म憭㻊䴧㚑畉箤ϴổྯ痷ൽ╡暕慩᱿涪敔净皱ᡞ沯揂፽╱懃抑綮ⳑ婮䊔嘎ḱ枮抄揹᫯ಮ䂖亇撩橭燅ⷾ檦硯筢卨Ⓐ䝕⊓疑ⱉ綪᪓棭Ặ楬ʇ剽Ṷ哖嗙ᶣᯁ术㧎ઃ᧞歬⧙ൾⴉ煬淍淸ᝑ晔᪉㐃ὅ╀洶⤳᪎痈皏㎢᧺峬ⷋ㵧᥉羬ⲇ劷᫚犨䬽ᔛự範皗⼘ᵙ僷予ᦏᵹ唬溄抯ᶌ⩭ƙ獯根糆纄珚⮉䱬ᚏኇ攥䉭䪋↨帙䶷⥶ກᢑ浘獫௙ᤎ繯媞஭句忮ኘ絝ፅ橭䦛௫⸨娒榀䭢἞䅬䦙⊬峥祌冁䮦䛅犗䬽ᓩܞᡎ㊇劢壄䣏↍文Ἦ圔▘⯺䙥罬䱡⭂忀昡₣Ꭾ᥄㠷璔淌幅棕牷⯼奵䁪䶜䨵䔥▊ᖔ⮮ổ䘢涊⯬崙烕斁ᕚ犕娄嶚琋ổ⏏ᶛ⤄勥㩧㖖仁富绍犐殐幕掊⎌欠徔秓ᓜ㷁ᔐฃ収単嫰暌޶㍿ᤕ歧玐ຝṭ厮砫ᯗガࢀ性ᡆ䟕䒍殁宺焙䱎斗緍෍嬮安ᰞ娉ྏ残㳗㉮ऍ榐䴬橢㤎嶃孥嬍畗➑寪壍夎ᮜ䫅幨⥇㡢㭼ᮥ✏㞌對妵紎䒄孵堾ᜌ⹌实徶缌⾖疧巛≏滉槊⫱硌璞⧏屍篌ក癏定䬌ދ筀湮䐡挷㮳ᨦ搾构篗䩎授ℋ໦䙔⡉ጢᄆ屠㈾滹ܪ⻐㤏䎋↘㴔קណࠄ棊房ᑤ䜤㽃樿儒悸㣍洽䤔椄十Ⱑᮋ↼㫧㈎⤁ݻ渃兀ᤝ塬㫣炿䥠ᱤ㸨含寋㵰ᒏ֌綻⛼㸨䲢⽋㴺㣀焗泶瘠˃⧦䴬箽⸉᧪籠瀲䍟ክႬ璆孝ᨕ䈼熇㯿盍俩†㵛ᷢ䯯ບ棿᳙槺䚅琒Ⰹ擮㊜㐓Ῡ竢憓罷ὺ噏擀b㞿筥ឞ㶫㩾̗➐八祈?䪷歴ᗦ⸮扷ဠ⃆Ż䋟አƘ疔⮾䡕獯嘲殽ᷨ翔⶜䯦嵡愆㵄䯾尲殛Ηீ弅燏擀^፼䱦㟅㣥㳿㌓埶冻祉␶㜡჻䋿汻㟫㩩羈㜚㟝㢫冹✈㟱㶈秽䜇᠝四竼伞搔壳ᒠ⼚ᯠ˾毼漅㝝ጛ祈4倗䷜⁀ὺ竱傘痡濍⨯到Ἒ猓ႛ䏸ᾂ瀗撜䐅ᙬ⚯ₘО倁窗㡷緾ṱ炖⊟䐞潑瀲㊝巟溭ྯ⟜仱䶉碈犜帊Ἁ縗⢙瓓ẑ粽噀␇瘢⿯懞墐庴禇䐥ㄵ嚕氯歹Ꮶᔅ熯〸Ҽ怀㺮ƛଘ܀໏ᆝ൮忥缷ా毹揕盭䫦Мű暏㱍氌ⵍ綏亜吂ȍ疠⫣Ⱂ↤Ս஝ᰇ忨盯ሺ小录悏燞㞀䀙劏咕䩍◝甿ᤙ渑㯕紿佨吒徽璿᤟ኽ傭尯洚ޛ滗垿ㆁࠍ濍⑿寔俖綡祿殗簁殯椏㔙埳ᩝػڛ滳䭻画㜸縕䍀ਈ⪩៯滜旿᜘࿫ơ翿෠俢㽩㗿᨝⠎᠇穛㙵唛盰㡏䲵〜怌⤫榒Ⰽᴗ璽囍⎴ÿ㞵ผ毠⒀ટ圸ⱶ窏皟䜚῍羐珞悟㎿ห綁倞䀑࿿疋㷵姗⿾匠沠৿佄㉨஀㿕㌀߰⻸㙰ᬑ櫡ă㗟疈儘᭢း忛䉈Ӷ朠☡җ㟺ދ⤿䁀⿾㐦拪⁰猄㤯旯⁍砮偝䜺疧摔ഠ歐ਃ披ƌѠ᳙ᜢ℅偉漼憭ր㱬‪氯ᓐỨ䁨᭟㊨刪⴦Ā䔄ෛ᷐ゐ㠱笭傍塰႖ઢ耖ѧℒ⡴ࣀڞ㔤穨ぢ纕篸䚀溢᪂塀悭͐牠㚼ᔤ᰻㟖䈖ݸᒆ㎢朵礱惃䒜ඐ⌴榨㰿㣏䡬狜䞥ঢ♀樤⸹˂䜨㡁ᜓ戴末૞ܤ❥c朁⑛Ô䉸劇ᾪ咧淯䡦↙ၩ₰痉┯ኴᢇԸ၈⣬⪥㻯侯㹻毴፰䪔椶嗢⼶䉦㔩᣸坃݌ߏℷ௨ᱰ掉̯瑁₦㖼䐈ⓘ灘怫ᑊ绞ᮋ①罼♀稾メ⤶ൠ⧁’昰塧ᒅԔ䛐廣ళɮキ䧅咨⁄㖧丸條繛݇浒㆜㇅ߺ檋䈦✈㬊㦤吼᳐䀿禜ᇀ俢竖汕兕䏞ഌ܈ĥ吊Ѡሀ䜁材壣爬屛ޘ⋆ਸ➡ᩘ儱吺ᄳԹ䛐䉂炯⨢䠫䑘噸ㄾ㖤ᴠ⎾ٺ҂乨兂栢Ꮂࣘ┆ࣄ㢱ɥ瞥呌偅䢥⩨朜欯㉂n⎋ᝤ㷰㦧礸ᒄ⪬䜱橈缑抨๴㍶ͱ惁ᛁ⦸ᔴ周愼嫊ᡟ㏣☐䋭e≺勉΄∡沃䷓湦ㄺἠ⛄ᘫ撢棾吮॑ᛱ悻Ꮑ⒔㳪䓗䅨⯃檬徲息⍅୨⏱橣䥤㹉ノ䕂᰸焄ᄂ穜᣿⏕฿䁄棦̾ρ傰梠ᮻⅅ䦮੆硥㤝ບ䍑̦⬬㐸碎䒝䁸冂庭㯰壨抓ഐ㓑䓤㎅䱐皫䌶Ᏺแ妦䣺棦楻ಌ⛾櫧澍仗ㆪଘ梠剂䈤ឫホ䏰਼⨁㡐帳楈煎ି敲ǁ䏖⻩अ挛㖨㶑᧺笲潁ゝ孪⍈坂斲≌⣃換炼㙌句Գ䑼ᑷ䗗䴈嵂⒭ᩑ佘⡹࿄㡱㟤᤻౽ġኞ፻⊱䀨忴á氠临≐偄漿浘ॐℶℤ剂倠䅋梤ኀ䲢⁖假╉结㇊媁ᘈ䳄䠱湚橜፧㏾䂁ቆ戸㐹৹ѓ≤湔殢櫧䣋糗熼ᡱ濸ℽ米廌⛽䞤嶨珰ㅑ掎Ꮻ☴⁩ⳳ洰ॐ䦑䈠ᖜ₲塩⯦㴾Ꭵ௾幩呄穨劀䧘歩ᒨ劲庪楀䒾䨄䤭䧶竻ȁు䥿笢ᥠ榳≬․撯⁏唩ა徑泃ኂ.▄䱈殲乪兜梴≼嚷䨐禤怩ᴿਁ⠾‴凘ᶪ整ᒨ愢䧧཰ᄡㄆ亸⧃堪Ẍ৵ᩩ╀桛緕ዾ尘奢劷湇倴䂔ᢏ঩㥯敉䶂Ǹส⭢〢⪼ᒍ⥀犲⊎ᴩ࿦ᕖ㣏ᤊ䳈㿰唧⪼ࣈヽ✪ῴ曨⊒䀹哵擺䧴ⓤ⇅ᠺसË䜕ဵ㤣晨ᶮ㓭㢺䮠׉㣠⮊媍沺栯͝⼳侨矺橝厨Z㡱叇亵㑚榻⑭᜸戡᝭⽦敖ൌƠᛖ㐡䀮㿆䚷穘柣⯳潬絞咷勾䣘倹毆䚱媘楸㨝ሬ䟳睗ࠠ憇ᏘѦ⯱撆≎ٸ槍▁暬䳲啇ġ䠨䉤㼹ݣ庍⒝䑄昳ቔ晒孨䯲䴀ⶳ嚓ڴ⟦匶㒒ⳣ䢎ը狲囶㍚䳨㋑仺⎹㡀䎁䊨ラUᲄ棒㚧୎哸䍛߁᩹঄ㆿ暍᥅⟚╌䳓∩坤䈾劮乀⌦ᶇԸ੺椰曽ᖧ㇓㞄丱䢀㳍䭆㮹ઇⶼ噹夵嫻ᾱᬢ啫歅゠䤕Šмࣅ䯋癿᧮摫搌囓ⅇ爢䂖ᆼ䢮⩙⽤掴๴ᤵ寧Ṫ⋃値堬亇፳䭟䍙⽥㎾乢㤢摫枼奙劰浗湘)慜ⳙ䑀৫䊕㤵搷ᫌ筲扯坄籑І䈼呱ᖆ␽䫇㧒䋡৔烃嘠睁撡獷ᎌʰ㵠䝁ⷐ禷䊯᷼嗌帐㒩ⴘ኷䳶Ⅹ㘅ᖼȲ礲摶榴ĝ䯬畜ݴ᷷互∠ᐅ㞿皙秦䊿ᷜ樼墖彝㴒⨕ݞ㬪剪঱ܲᅏ树֛ࠓ湨㨧紗狠Ҭ‥懪懡⷗福暅ఢ淹၏㽳ᑪ父佔‥汋䬡M㨞无嚢涓⁈䘼ʩ㳐⡡㽂䤥޵㊜ᦤ曙ĝሪ声攩ŋ玈⫒⊥瀩ⶅↇ妨箰⒤縳汫⟹䌄痲䟚ᄉ嚄弿浟׽䆹ჹ╈〣吼籫焭ǰ୺墢綻檨炯匲ވ␑䘵♺䜰Ť⯬଼嵄䱫农˗㊳ᵁそ♌ᙰ〈㇘ŐԠ碢ᆁ懔梖ዸ徂糅睡循ァだިເ敱㟁㆖ㇼᔄ⡬妫擂䮬S஼伩㉅晻Ⱳ煣䔴慘妢㱪湎瘣拆ࣗȑ⿥欫≹㆑ီ ἴ䖍㥊䩹ᵇⱂⳑ⤱犴承䆼▖ᑄ坤⚱䥏哕ዜ懲⶚୅洷⩷䥡䔡᎔婲歴⅌哚䊾ᒦⱷᛅȀ砢䥴ォᕔ凈㓫湈侳括䮜⻱ㅪશɳᲄ槷禬宖ᤨ᭎Ͽ㊺䯾砎൨ֶ晴祙斍ᕌ冲夡ᵊ৷㌅ቬ≙ヒ哒Ṵ䑹䂯ᛤ奒䶪ⵉ䳑勫䬞ⱹ㣰斵湺奶窿ᐼ匸Ū㎣嵇磤Ł⴩㥚ᴣ干ᦕ呈啢帒姪䃈峏䩋䬭މ⯥箷ⱁ䕬☇䇘塲届伕ዕ猄璶敥ⶥ丛楹䕤旸囘怒侀獋䀿ૢ⩶⻩㗂晵䥳ձ┲稪孪桨ೊࣘ瓣䉹⥙⻅癶ᱵ繓┪嗄厒䝫惉翳૾䯐灙⠢䥵¶䲞㉿ᛒ啒乊瑢⫞㋓⨩⭵⢵൶婅吶啡ᖈℊ剋⅄␿⬏厠䥑᷵奴簊㦉啊垺堪悋囉˖狶ᆩⶈ䟵ⅴ⥻ն໱垪啲Ⲙཱི⋊䭒᳒䣟ː䬡塯Î⁴䌒庢ᠤᩈ恫⋋ↂ䇷឵ጠၭᅄీɨ嵂䘐牯䣖ѥଏ䊬ᒸ柒溤㐫灒Ø⤤⮝୧侸墙祻⇴˰⸋፷湖喳咸嶸Ⱃ晋仒আⳓ⧭⬢糴浼为䕰̶奞⦊‧ᛌj毋Ⱡᕥ竴摴浢䕪៖师ศ巏ἷ媻∛ⴔ႕ᝋ岢ᶊ琿㬳ଶᚉੲ⻛⪿氇⨬㨠嘧暸斃१挡卛㸬⯊䀷ᬕ櫣⬒Ԩ电怩兹䉐燠ź䜊嗎☴窯※ⶱ㧕⫱⽺穭疋⇾叺律٫碼ऐᗿ⦂ᐕ⸈⃻Ζ煮圤ⓦ䠻㣮⢽䜀㷘氱䘭㡖⤠⵺ᣨ㛁弱㨻ᢈ⇆⒌᪋⬈໕㱗併㹁෍坈婦䗱撈㻉笊ᪧ⮝㌐凷ီᶕ䋜㘦ୈ╼⋋⭁甀ᮀ⽎᧩揣ᇬ嶆僋嘆塆䜋׉ৄ嫔᫫⣣ㄕⱗཻ䍴䔪㗨妚宊⒏ᴠᢊɈ沝⪭៶棻卧甦㛔⮆籘〥ቫݤ宿䲱ა㐢✪ȭ䴹㔆බ稃ၷ燍㬇᭄泽⣕ᑗ島ᎇ䴲㝌嵆䨋Ԣ潨桚਒槫⯩㡳᫹䭡ⶪୁ尯ջ⑶ᗉ曁᪰滽㋍巴㳿嵷䵧唁壶疥綊㳂歾宿䶢٨木匰㕻᨝冋⫖激Έ㧖ڲ宦榬෭燗⫹ᮍⴹ៵卂፺⮋樷㚥婼䷛ⶍ⚉䔉Ή涢ᡵ婆皺犏科嫥᪢楳㑍㈣䋱却ⵔ㜮嬶紻熈㚼寬沃䘍ⓣ䮸䅸ෟ▩沮椵ᾊ嗛盓欞氫◕扔㭻㵨ᶴ㐮帮人ᠣ槁䛈ᦁ橧⛙≣᮸䁃ุ瞲䷠ㇵ䨂⍝仢婏拧㔍Თ擷䝲䶤盉嘶瞋ℋᏛ皺᫉溧㖔無㧰枖斨Ǔ僕㊘礪ፕ᫈䋉䰱娠燖䀫ᑚ䡼ᄜ庢౛笎ⴭ⢑᣽ۑ⃘᎖䐽ɐ䆖䏸䭈ἠᨨ嘨擊ࡲዷ㰠㘳塥䏉ᥕ姐䉢ڬ䪰绱䓶ࣀЯ㌽Ꮤ䜦㮐礴䏥༰⇀䴢໌呪桅劝凔❺疩㰾夎甝徦䘊Ԏ׈仒ᩩ沫≽埴塧⎋僴疱䋢唴㏌Ẩ箿䥡㠾䠶⏺᭷洵盧妀㲛਎⟕t竏㐱ᥤ䴔㮳侙ࣘ琱倮瘊䄍ㄴ廭ᯂ梧㊽㣕㽻ល㴤ᛗ幪㔁㰧㷘䲻↗橬ϝ᷷⏽筯㶝畇包છ࿣⟚筜䣧滯㙢䨔׽ᾁ㶠痈⻆楛俏Ꮢ廨㯋榷⺸Ḕᇷ♡紨睪Ⓒ⬜彮߇瓺㣮䨔ぴ೵伥ཾ畳琷呦冚⌎ό⻏竔棏⩽嘕ᝆ椤̨ో徔尧ှ硓䒃煼䘠椱⸑⡓ậΐ砀毮樚ᘍ₟盗箇椟↝ゖ◵⽸疋痳ཡ䘢䟢よ纩㱤Ề樠〯Ꮒ焬䎛璋倲㲧䀾㋵䇝毯榠ŝ䰖札㾆僣瞞ਫ਼筙搊㿜ื竰ṳ㮣件硞⽬ⵋ畣呁䊱倥⢑亵ݾ毨㋠娭ᑒࢥ჊೐㲡䓻ᨾ梀㼂₧潯⣣ⴕ〪ヾ㴡㔫冡崛​៛缞ܟ氰炣੤屘坦␎ཇ⩸ᚘ䢫撑ǒ倢᭛⎣粗偞羕䏸ൄ㮡嶧匌㢌䁢䝨ᾥ⧃丒珡㟛⌿㒴㿮濻〈咊戂㯊᱿⠝簬᱘⃠繨੓兑圳ᖧヽ㛯⬭⩓֍㦯࿶᭻͗↴㜱敧̿廇ǅ穉濈炣斯ự៑換㚏佂ኁᒡ栦䐺䌈᳘檰ᮮ➻㢄ଊ౭姑䴚↉炈㇞ܐᠰ罭ڮ墡棆Ư໼㇡ᓦ༾岌৥戾㝼Ḥ㘘㛼ᅩƐ䷐䫑垚ᬿᢓ䈞䛞᫈瞃᪯癛羝䐟瘢㧡஥⢸䯣摒⚁ἠƼ疖击䗍ᎈ侃廡晇攼墇ঽ䙂游敃≭剓❦⣹協㔏Æ೯ݏ⁲ℴῄ止繣䕜惩斏ິ㫩囦̹ះ燻޷汘暽ᥬ║ᄙ䷺䴄㨲㜠纤䪊⬝㉬≔濣祯㩒攏⌶༫傱䶧䤻粕ᆠ✨ᣔ渽䚗嵔㽻⏀斘㕉礄Ґ哗⨟ݛ溄挳孭ㅞ攑㶊㙚㭱䛆й叔䜯卒Ὶ⥓⃯憹ᰱ碞人㘌戡ᦼ媏檥⚚`㉓筯㹗䔗Ꮾ伒㬉䵛禸窑⻚柝ᠵ䥐ᵭ⁑Ⲭϊ䣖㝉憇嚿ڄ姖⛫ᷤ殳徭橐䴍㶐໖㑉媜Ꮈ᪊剘ߓᱤ穵啹ጠⳣ㉥䳺㿹狆Ჽ⪂妱栃ᬸ暽积歖⃪珓佈䡱攇乨庛姕枛ᩄЃⸯ㝓೺卮亮゙涛垽檑仯栁䭘籰䯭⮿º涷䷈㞙妦ᆸພሒ枧ὴ愃㇬懷糨஬癁㚙䠡⤀ƛ戔ᚏᶘ氫᢮׹礔㏂眎㬥慇᪽埋׏朵棂縹咒几峢掻㝺䭥欆㡽ڏ亭枂ᡂ猣稔彗೼ఏ䳣峥爇烊উ姰䦈壢翳൐ⓝ䋯ᷘⱞ㶩愶堾ᆕ稝枩᱀晫䩏溹勦㌧癩㎹扜㰉Ƅᦳ穰ᩴ殫ݮ磐┈搊⻶㟅炶伒ᦕש憘ǖ㗫⺭壞夝理⹞㓅伶⩻熔䘘ច榒睼圮峚㡬=䏱㴡埊圯固ᗹᚰᴒ泫ࡍ㝗猂⎵䷞㮅涛㙬▋☘⬒墬ᙣ傳摨勐牑⿖㜵䡤汐慸嗄垪ᥪ縃὎ᓝ挆⮛們㎵䱚敻喅ᨘ⪚壊甫㓬⡜犐歄ಙ㪅獶楸妚ؑ㭴崊澳嬕䛖乴獧爦ㅡ紥点ḣ]䑄᤼⮋᧢盔⤊Ēⳕ㔹孷ㆾ妟熺突楜ඤ淍໚嬛䈧ⴍ㉵劋椊᪍盄㭞墺涃哎㝓᫰玓⸥㎅拶ㄎ㏇瘘㩞堹㸋⒖桁㰲器䝓弭双䲿㆏姮វ壚櫫ᆯ⻐àヨ湀₭号䄴᎞梂㚌坧㼤ࠠ⼦洀૵⽓嵭浖棺禜֠㛑峒恋⯌嵓㬌嶬滿ͭ澨⓸ժ䶡㞹峆椽塁бࢗ䐜潫㋭翷᣽㖓䶸᠆娪恫㺎䗟ᛤ庒泐ᚑᛀ岕඀渑୸岺煳槌㧛᫾揘洓㾭夡լᮜ暧㜌俔䥐皒⫟✂掐凎׈─ⱻ䦉嘓㟹并櫻籬淝ⴏᮔ愛㼍䎶樖䞏淴ហ⶙¹㩬೙徲㬴䈛尕穇幸宄᷀㟍娄沫炍㽂伐孜檷㠎朙亄℣淕ᕗ盭ཤ羏ዖ㜑㍪澽㋍灗峸䞎淀⚋嬕䃋䄧篖笒䓍䱢⤧ቂ揹㌤涠睻夂缫䮌௖໱㯡ⷳ՝渀处㏝㸞ၽ岪㒲泠巳繌庻ዛ唵簒瑊媐ᷖ瘷忮玳⼏䏜⼌嵘ᪿ㢝擧଎㾀縓睍䤤槝ℕ⫕真㓳䁠㽾䋖卾ރ巰盒孲氻჌習ǨϠᾧ傈犩儫狤槥曭Ḝ㱁朎᫗Ủ᭗池瓝吮୹嚖廴༚媗岧呍桮䩚ܬⵂ㏲മ㡙ᶊ縙眚᱁漛䌍⭘绽ᡬủ㭮Ἦ扺⛔ⳡ੐㷬爠ᄪ䂔༛㮣亐糝眯⯸ᎄ␒瞲晱摖瓀朧嬗䎋䋐惵䬮硝果Ϲທᵶ搻㲌䥓分䞝扗凃樷Խ㾘ྛໟ廮汓䌼撕˱ܽ⿋㗵泚九ᙥ␞検㩞竛盢塶伃਋⮻Ճ瘗汞ᤙ秎㘿山绻瑙忚䳪⟪ۜ䢜⨙乪怠籯姂㮁滳༽撜∗䝐ᷳள噯噜⯒吜亠ោŪ䩱匬牣Ⴍᱰ偳縯ㅞᔄ搛癷壶溸嚼怤槣㶪瘬籓扛䫷䲖ᖠ࿍⒃䶺熶⿐ㇻᰎᾌ㏳圯奿ᔀ䷑Ḇ㠩皇涾፴猸仡䃺ʠƀ壒⎈现慮㭠ἶፍ绖Ǫ杊俤窃瞖㱚洅始仮㷹檶䮼井秤家Ϩ娱Ꮜᮦဦ簼憨ǐ઀⿎Ɵ吢ᯀ徢瘘ᑏ煩㤝෗ศ㮩梫ើኟ樛某弢琁ᡏ堢⌚஽㛤爥縷ሢᆙؔᜠ廀穃紮䮸ұ䞚⹚㽥毇喿ẛ槢䟘嶰˫硣᯼⯟䮰֎捏ţⴽⓔ㌸埬ᶎ哓帶᳚㴋ఎ⹖㵁昽楿碕僚坢ṥᄫ嶖∈㫸䯧坱㶆繷⊾㦔嘚柰Ị甝懎ᑙ烖毛ླ嵆㙰ܤ੔瘁᥎巒糓䙏嵚猒殲གྷ堬ዛོ尽紛垀ʚ炀恰ᢖϣ濤癕煻὿䶜化ឝᴘ煳粏⇙唋ᯓ䗛⯵揓燫玗刌堗Ὠ粻拏⧞⬊毠瀍幍炛㔘ᮂ簨筞䃸恻畷ᳬ碄尕杚㭕狗罍厓旦㜡䊖瞋氤淞㦔Ǒᵽ㼐栣槽㶚㘉㏞屺罃䫏㗞Ⲫ㮸湠ᱟ㱮ᭊ㺓㧳ℍ㍙ᴎ痮⾤ἁ㮥ᙘ㭹疗᫾篞^瞇崾缮䐏柚h梃♅㼩燦㥨㾜㬉㝙澚烋吆⯝ᔔซ⸦㾝沗杶℘仰寧巡稥欯㷚⼅ᮡ濋㠭漗偳⪟㩶༵私杣瓯౹璴➀朶㭍晇㻿ĕ⸟垅ᾡ瀸ि墟䋁䟜Ἰ瘹㉷羋焔䰾▗ᰡ磛搷⢟㖄䗐ῷ㴧Ꭿ䬡牸杣༧ẩ畎ԙට兝䠞楰疳磰祜⾖㬆៴㳾熧䥇䪙母➩㴔箳簘ؓᏊ䎺焌Ꮦ獓焿䚠娜⯟溛㾅犯೎⻓䘐瞄ι瞈㶿彘㉶柏ṻ㵣帠ཡ猥㏱࿞㴥电娯⒙皉߇Ṱ耍灯㖏ԗ㸀⿏ብ甧灥⦞؊᠘㍰煻ぶ朽ᄷ䰅〥䀘碻䏮ᗚ刍޺ᾲ緳磰糜䌬爙䷥㰯ࣷ羮⧪枉ࣴ㣓屣湷䯾㔝Ⱆ俔㲩緷柛഍ด⧊䤈塃耛ボɭᰔ⿗以砧玿壸┝ᯭ仨{熯➛㜛㭂冀ᚥ烣䦨ޛ惆⯧Ṷ羫櫏䓝䲛㛩Ꮗ㽖燋灤ྙ㜆䶷Ү窅笮в梘尉射㸴疗䮾㣸渎䞼מ磫稊炞僘㶻ᴌ၂⑷瘍ㄟྜྷ⟜盏㰕梏嫞ࡓ߱ቃ´ᶯ属啧偮䉇⇥䴌ኲ࿄朙盼瀁⌳穯䐡攟Ḕ痴㸦秛瘇Ⓘ墢䁍ᾀƳ縤ў䚄琙桚㸹絢恿ኟ㨘䜗䏂緳犯冯䯚樔ࠓ༨᪷籿὜ⶅ标オோ罯䨲⎪氟剃注縃翏㦞ܐ埽潪縋犤离䬛ᐆӂ㼥缷祀乙竷堓怅㾶琧偟殚༓㞮㽽翿嫿羟⥕៨᥾㙳罽挲∝囬῿徇怛礯繜ጚ珨ὂ㵧煸Ė㮛⟭Ᾰ老䪷纰ẜ⨙緸䞨稇灿损䮛爝ᗕ弧㭽漗匟樛柳漺㏷籏盏䒥吟ᾩ㼴绕ởᦞẝ㰒㽞纣砏惟ḝⰆ俱繕翗撿伟瘒砄翺罠᯷粞熜⠀䀀㺧絯揟宝᠘杫㾖罇⋿察㬘〉澠纘綑猏㘝㸓」睄䴿瀿弟尟吙瀉縱❩ę稜䨒㊆㳍ѿ皫嘞⬝᷸欔Ⰳ❪⾯罯縲秠ҟ煘⢟嚿㹾〜け᠗耂㗸澠佡绕縏篠ो湟䩿ȡቩᘓ䏰縉䇱@⼠笅級碉煗櫯䷯⿞兜封ࠪ㠎㪰䁩ж滌ᦊ⁒瑃沗妷⻬᥀㏸寑〉嘿㉏㵍ܝ瓏樯凟₁弝ㆦ䠕ģῶ㐍⁃}罢܌̘ޯ異ቦ䰲㙺㴰–㐨珌忷䞰⍑ǚౄࠈ㜨殔٠呦㤣&Ǒᔅ燳ྭᶖ㣴֑稵㏰Უ䩈➎猵ḧ帓ῌ၂纨⍱抆̏梇哐ᅞ䛠挖㬢䊚䀫ᄍ灜曝ၯĦԔ⊐ර淠⺼ቡ׼䘤瑓Ḧࣸၤ⌳۶͋竸ໝ暏䟛ॆ朣˛溷ᐿ䢦捄䄺䅞ϛ樘രᖰ⽣⸚ሔᘦ≓и⡂႑ℛǱʁ櫤ಇ₰ⳅ㈬栤啈䘨ᰃ௮⯆₠䅙˺џ勐ᮾ䴠办ฝᠦࡒ怯户㾭➑䆎旤稟㋇檰⼍᭺ᐢᨺᨮҎၔᇄ䄓ȓ͚Ռཿ渏喀䵚䎢⸥Ḃ㰻䎻䁁〯紏И܀琰ᛱᥛ㾡玣Ħ娬ᢎ桟ႂ惊Ȉɶ݈ಐᘐ㲟㬴ྣ佪另ᨤ汩ඬ炑⃨䊍猼న檐㣠癡䮣㤦䄭䠾с₄ᄛ䇰䎋欈睤ᓸ帽ᩁౢ䳱儬䀤Ⱶࢊ㱦↱䓑ӧ凤ᳰ㓠灁椢ᴧ≕尳㿽ߐ潬Ḭ䍝又ഴᙜൺỡझ㽩倦珀ၐ悇Ⴙ䈘䌆ڤငᄨ㦀奁ᵜ⨥支⠻呚⼩兏湁Ⓧ਻瓟栐⹝፡敢䄦唫爰⡀⢕㽁℮΋桶Ӵ䣮䗰籒砡䚠㉶␿塓矇儏ℹʵآමረ㬀竁ባ᪦瀖樸䳳㈠ラۑ䍗̏㞔໢ଉቂ灨坨ఫᨽᡘᡪ僰憊䌍Ҋ௘ᔸ㡰䥆瓣篳䳳ᘴ䱆X偉悑啦壶໚ฐ㽧⿡波☤⸮娷䱖梑ჹ㻄䎫՚ধ⵸㛐䩎➌ඥ捱❊䜹悐Ṻᚳ䐊ӽ֌ឨ⏐潁っ爤第䘸瑏傌嶉慚ʫ䡮ৰṘ㛰㤤⻝⤀༨徉ᡅ塰ブ慠䋄Ҥଌዘ㿟⃁ဣ朘槵冂㱜㾫烤ѥ䢷䪄֏ⴄ徙᳈濣珊朮悡㱁㡯Ⴛ懫䏢ۿ㈈ᔰ⨐珁⿢㾧䳳縺爠ґኄ璚䂍ㆇ刔ፈ㘢՞ᤢ䶧羒昲Ʌ傕烜䅤䌏ٵ炜ᆯ䎐䐾ృ獠⨯䋎䉁纲・Ú播ݶ⃷࠸䀀旁᳣஧䂫ᄹɍྨཾ䇐⊁棑༿晄⒲Ḛ杄俑ª࠵扌炅炰慫䐘䖔ઢắ䓀寮ཛྷ剧ᬓ忍彠纭妝ᇒ⏭Ҩࡲᨤ⒨慁֣摦㸐㨸籔傁̽笃簼䐹ᄚⲄ䢒᷒◜匥ࢮ爾㉌ᡡエ慥䏷ҩභ⊄䗨䕆㝂♊籕瀲⍹撦⍈刘≎笹ࠤᣄ㝐犱䭂ɤ娒⠽ౌ䏄⢮ȃ綂䜅ऐ数♈䕀⋃ᦤ,┽扙ᒏࣲᆉ⍴䘩ྷ汄⻨䵚੥╦᧱㔾䡄䤼ハ⡳⮗癃旴⇇㿴㋂⛛朮ᄵ㡟ᢗㄛ慖⋈䔥ெ࿤ᯈ僱䥜ͤ窭昌婑⑒ 䂠┹㢰ྺჳ嶈曱乂ᚦ䲫ര⑗撄梪ᇳ≔䟓甧۔⣰۱㋸䭧㪯洺″咗⤌棏䇅ࠊ症௔㺊߱䏂♦焩ᴳ㑂ѽ⢬兰䋒䓣刚ἔ㙈㤞⢃ⱐ憭㴰槮ᓇ棢渺ゞ䝃ယᒴ⳨磱寣楦ᐯ̲ⱋ࿒梬ㆦ㶩䛫Ѧᒣჰ熞丘㽧崬挹⩛ಉ梩其⍶笠঺ᓴ㛝ⵑ㭥ⓧ㪫匱♜䪧ᖊ糫∥䒐扒ᩔ㯨乑ႃ皥妪崻旵䐯梱ㇲ᤾䑔瑶ዃ೯㋱⇸〣摒ର婅孖壑ㅾ⏻֡৊᎐バ攱妃溛斨欷噑翂崿冺揕䑳జ悔㩨狱枂ጤ㲯ḿቐ౤壆㇘捡䠃૴ᡬ⚽࿱瞃ュ嶭䲆孠瑥ᣇǻ䊪筍ථ῀㶰澡澂岥ඩ礼晏ಏム儼捁䑇ஐḼ㯈抑眢㽦岡ؠ䉿㽜㤎内挍Ћฺነ㕘嗁掂ᙦ䶯社㙑咆䣋ㇵ扳ѷଶೌ㥀එ异ᘓᚬ༿ჳ糗䍲煝拧䟳๚ᰌ㠸䪱榃ၘ㮮崹Ṝ岔碾ㄭᵧ䝠ό╲ࠈ坢ѭ学獓漽⡥熼㽥↭折䝗୚ዬ〿◱昂狤溮甿幐屣➇焴抇շࢉ捘㻘癁ం啥⾬朰๛᲍䣮熯拟䞎຋泔㊐发䤃瞊㾪′壠汿磦㈓掊䙏഑挤㝘泚儃うᗧ眷糸㲗⣴狋㒒毠乁ቬ⠘䝁搲䃦㬪䬶㙎粆Ӱय़⏨⛫þᲰ֤疴疂䑇嘃Ⴓ垹ᱣℊও授⑏࿁ፌ㼘旑〳汄瘇眻⋰䉣❺ᚌ椃䑯๺Ⴢ㰘缩㧣ۥ⼬䬲ᅍ屣ӄ廴␈磈䫗东♤熩㷢屄᪗稰ȵ汻梤慉秴✡ఱẼ㭤娩儲䯦ᡩ⼼婊扪㺞燾፶䞕࢟⏌Ⱈ䲡ᨂ㻧ᱫ笷⅗≸䒯य択䘤䮁ᠲ☤倶彡睥ɨ₶孵ቲӃ冁ዔ⑤䧱᫘⁈䠩伳嵥罔撹ń劎Ӵ䤴抈㭰፩፲⭁Ω㥃奅厭撺䅕屡┖煑ቄ┝࿉ᎏῘ潩㤲睰撧䊆䥒䦨擌䤠扺╉ంᬂ⩄箩紳㍦౨ⴲ䓯屽墭ㅋጦ◮牏梜ㄾ࿱ⶲບ烗ା्劘ギ䦚ᎎ禀䮺ᛔ㎗⚞濃坄瞔ಷ≴㊓ऩ䥸抈⛅ྉᕔ㩄䋩䮲䭆ک㲾⥟犉佹咋⊽㎿ͩᶶ䜐ⷮ卣敥๭㒼ᅖ㉹攏䤷ኸ⚢䪥ጜ㊲ᡉ墐ᓥʓԍ♑䒯棼⧁዆Ⓟহᨒ⌈牉㚝ㅇᚪ኶慈䩮ᒯ燪Ꮪ䙲ͱጪ⒈暩榲⛦乪粿᥅ઑ⒦乌剀⠗వᫎ䋤䟜綰楇缢⫩ⅅᲓⓆ焹搝䟀䲨ᐒ㔴冑ॲ汅╬಺¼ഽ℘৺厂ٔ䣊᭜㤄䉉牳噦⥭值ῲ⊞哚䆠刴僀ǵᷠῤ斩䡬楇Œ岌╞⩫䓓⧌掙╲伉ᘂ㗴嬩睳እ䕮砿ŀ橻ᒦ熒协䑊䲩ᒪ⿴旉ᅝ棦浯眴ᡄ੥┄䦲䆎匊慀ڲ㷸牠峲ụ缗ἳൟ籼㔜䥜剐Ⓤ倅Ẳ㟰⛱䋳᫑獫グⵈ媀撫䐼灱Ւ䢉懺㪐♁⣳㿥䭩₺㕛䩥ᓤ楉籲筍ญᵨ㿘甉㞘拆䁃㪷癠㩵Ӂ樏ዩ⚮何Ṛ㎟┉㟂ℂ籫݋幍沉玍䥼͞窧ढ़႒⋟᱉乲ⷦ㝭窽ⵏ䪕ᒲ䦷剑┾㎏惌⋐ᴶ㑢楄䭆毩⑓檌㔏⨗厏䑺䢽ᯇ塸堉R汅置纽Ꮺ౦灴眘匼ぁ䦷䬒↸笉⹲繤፬㺿畎䂊೐嚋ዾ䙁䰹᧷寔弴睂◆ࢪ㢿Ճ牨ഋ缇ጐ敺䨚᏷忘喖ㅳ੠嶯䂹捘婹礊ᦋ劤◱代ᕺ㥴吉ò佥ഡ㬷㕇䚛㒮ᅖኛ◩䦵၂⁬䧉⅓来㝭憴䵗㩢䳭㣓剘䑳੢ႜⴔ仱⧲䯪ïᚼ͘♸瓭ᨀ㊩䜓୓ᛢレ惩ണ䤛擯୅੕晲䲭॔㎏❿૮ᛘ⣄琉ڼ⺄ᅃ媲୐侸咭Ɖዂ柁乕᭦⎔喹൓⊅ᣮ⚼婆ᙸⳈ冣ᐗდᙣធ㦴䔬䍲㟆䥪憾十窒ⳍᤰ㐒攳䘵᱌䱴壩㘱෇㏲洼㍈粚攁䤭㋻⛥䧩ᰆ〤勉桂㗅˪ವ⓱噶'兤㐞⟕䢉ۺ⊸绑湓栘坭䪹᥋橾ⓤ⥂㐚斩俣ᛔ㛸幞ⷓ咸穬㊷橁䥒梲࣌勯ڶ䩻ᐦ▌俉偓寄Ḭ猼㭄折泇㻰ዥ❘ඓἢ⸌桹䋒᳇૫庸䭌嚚沴姺㌴♁ԓῼ㐌䑹ೳͧ悗䂻综暐瓕ᥗ戸斡䧽᥶㨼刮౲焄⦭㈽ୌ⡷Ⲳ⧵⌞暵䧛ᎆ㔼嶹惒礅䋫਽䝖䡷㓣夡႞䙲௄ᾮ㦌䧩習┇䫭妲ํᚍ᳞䥯㊹旋ધᾊⶺࡩ㝓嫇扪禸煅⚜Ⲳ奨犠۽佄ូ⾔䣙ⴔᣇ䗩Ҵ䥎㇝梱姭吀⚴䢍᧶㉼卩௒ᚅ⻯冿᝔乽泅㤭ḕ攆䪍ᙖ➌暉ⶒ܇淬ಹת㡄⎜槮⁙悗ឧᦦ⢼峙⊣橧䑬液⥛溇岶樁玝摳࢞རөੑ櫍◧敃䞴㡁㚒䲳㤨爲朳乧჎∸瘩ሃ䨇㝳㗏湖ṱ㴗ƥ⑅吝⏀暱ֈ忙䅒娆Ϯ琼ཋ剽ª秕獄᣷䬣䫵ۜ䄩⎌ᒡ歨ⴆ㭟䙦㴟㦞㊠␥來ᨢⷜ澙➌㸆灯殏潝㒖Ⲯ䚫猎䝏䦇ᦖⶼ皙ஓᴅ䧬⚃⽉㹥ى䘧狷曵伏᫞ヰ♩欒᠅䩮綳獗癸糞姭爦摨䮏ᴔ㲟ᰙ㯃凤毁垾㢼⡙Ἱ㜔玽猟两䗔\"嶙啒ง糬ᒹ὚瑻㳟稀ਜ਼栗䡠壄Ɯ䓔淔瞉⚑␷瑆幦ʳ䙦犭➕䢟᯶ⷤ旙䖓㌉寫恿㭶㺟㳊Ր涛僷䶱៾≺ጥȪ䖆৬㾺⃗㹵岪֬௄♋厏ᭂⷃؙ瘓堄◄⤮彍䅯沮Մଆ▰⯯᱁䔜懀䤫䠄䑋᾵⤭繭撵稂૔ᒏ䵗ᗞ㇜媱⅂⸅⵬桰祉Ů䊧䧢੅勋ఠ囤⁓㾙嬪ဴ旨޽Ó剫糶祕犼ᑸⱍჲ应稙উຣж桱瞨㥐⋝ֹ玅旘ⲃᅶ㲃඙₪紆南䑶ࣟ慦䋮祋ን杕仠剠ⷜ絹⧓⼄≍ྻჇڗ֪̒ఛ昄⳨刞㵂擹⪫嘴ᓅ罋䚗䎘֭ஏ旇伓ᵎ⟌拉⸫Ć扏澼䃍兴䳵Բ栰ស䠨啂␼䊙歝恑硊䱼烛农㓕姯牖暸⮸外⥂羙唳晄♋摲࣏ㆁ⌚祱௧擠⣖ᨁ⋂䛩Ἢ笷橏ਫ潌→⁻䘓献ᙠ⹘唞㣢䞥㖫縆Ṋ暽⣋煡Ԛ䔨୤ᓔ⤠卑৐㨄⺅ủ仫㲴㣕慩挗׋੤竔ⴤ嘡╢䂥ၫ兣翮⾰ӑ冓⋀ը䩑ᕩ䯟ᗱ㢢佥㤫┴ᑈد䓉塐拔▣றឆ䭠屎ⶐ㚜䛠ᮡオ紴㢷繣唆╰᎟΄僑⒲勥歓撷Ϊⶅ擎甫ጞ◐㡦ᕒⳠ⯩㖲䒲–縆淪呼惀㺖峣㥤䩧擢ⴀ噩⿂坙煪⪶⩩㮴歗煤婵◳㎵ᚬ⨭ᾑ⑔孁ສ匄畉㱻Ӎ煣⢳֨䮟攦䧀厉␳༑ث䚵㍭承ツ礼糀旜㈵ܯ交匉⽲䥥ͪ簅ൈ婻䅆䦆拄昁䬹ᙦֶ⾑㍒猉∓デ⑈ºⓎᥪ拀㥄䳻攆⽔停≐ሒফே啋噵პ繬䋂旫௾ᑂ⯝漡㾔浅冫߄͉ふפ䊔挊㺢ਧᑰ仴崹◢沅囫溴㹌穵壔㦋ҿ☌ሷᚐ䢸囃άࡥ痪檫䝈憻哘冔狳㹁獞ᑫ⋼崐㇗඙叫ಶ淩ѽ㳙熄猝敂䰃ᔐ⽈嚹㧼䏙硵各䵉㴽㓀㱼祐৓ᘞ⮸䣹㢲玅慪䦅ὋᑹⓆ幨禟文䫶尗䶢划ᬲ絅Ⴊ耆ՋŹⵑ祩㌞䖩䨺ᛁ⨐庥㻂殉ʫ眴䣋᩷㳑ㅶનᕘ⬭ᐮବ坑哲棹䫫摷ᣏ呺䃝⥧રᗮ䰏ᓖ⻢囹㓒履ఓᖶ偉ⅶ䋟悮狘奴⭶树⦼廹Ⳓ䡅䫪䄨ŏ䌴᳕ႜ˵ᔸ⬫ឡ⠧᭥⅒紵搫᩶࣌楾拒♶⋿⅙઴ᘲⲔ岎⊒璵毒㨇摋ੰ㋜ⅹ䪱ᖎ⨬ଟ懩昅㮪嶵Ⅻ呶瓈ॻ䋆ໆ㶚ᅮ祢堄⟼䇈৿⻬獋塧ᵲ䕽䊥䴮癿ᗛ䪃ᑞ⧂吵⺪泚椉具ዏ㹲硑ᕬ⬎ࡠࢪ嗒⯆漵ㅡ᥵Ჹትࡌ慳ዓᕼ䫡ᖯϊ咴搸᫵㸹⹵婈䚠徰⨂ೈ昷⪼ᑝ⨽Ģᒤ唹ⵊ漵ᵊᴆ⃈剶‰㖎੾嘃縆圭⸘⩵⃈⊩捡ᒠ⫈牵⫝㕸⋍啺⩋⑕Ⱚ哵㡊乵⋋筶湨╷嫘㸡櫕嗧䗜ᦕⱚ妆㮜備ⳋ穷介笢๱ᖄ⬕嘜⇖囃࠺呵䀊珵㎓洆᳍੿汓疔⪰㗿⬞嘠⍢ᰭ㍈ᘥୋ㦺ۏ㽈Ὄ㖞㋆旺⨢坭⯲崙⒗ቕԐ䭷৏偳琨啾砸傲Չ啿䔦傁㩂䩙䊊獶槎卷ۚᕵᬌ⦨毶哹ᘽ䢨刊兵床㦣ص啰❗එ欜㘏⮹囑к呍㲁㦺妋♫稷嵽䊹悖Ժ㕗⬨ℰ哂怅≺䑕᧋乷⇍⭷ऻⵢ媫商毰⬝⺪幩ᶱ᪵保ʹ淏坪䫊▎媧ᕛ爭啣⠹摵ㇺ䥴盋歴総㠸᫐᬴牄≡櫝㉶䟆剚㰺篕ʊ側姏⵼ໞ֕欈喩櫍啠厠ʭ㋊纄⒊᧶⏌⎸曗ẁ嫏㖟⩋Ȁ䴹掽㲺惵䳬᫷⋎坳回啻嫗嗇⯒圷ⷎ孼俺宕㔋惰氡…澨ƀ欌櫝氅Ԝત兕㻪秙✋޴㵋开ệ嶏嬒瘋⬧埆拉ࡕ↠䤨屈䬫篊ᕶ廃㶘煊᧸歠垫Ⲏ哾⩺岕ᦋ寴ϵ潺⛝㕮竝࣡粧槙ᚒ▘㈚珕㫊䟴⟉ὼ滃畽ᢇ疾┗硟⯒佡२吕总⿵䗊ᵼ㻈慷笉㗊㋀Չਡ奀⤘㐪㻔䐉ႌ篊ᛕ乴㫷喿櫇囮⯏檣㤦尭䐻䡖姴柌޻䀹ܚ瘏毃噯⧀ዽ㐈┭獔ᑗ姥嶡⇓Ҳᅖ෇䋑埒䧦儣␚吭尻牵嵗彮ῳ䎍沑₴᪱ࡨ榁啣⾦䴭᰺瑗㿈حᇚ湃ᴵขᩤ㝙Ⴑ厤䌦朙ⰻط檬ࣼ櫖廖䛴伐啬㖼✤ⲍ⛙᠀⩡䨰ᕉᨁ㞪捴拣㒖᫅᜜ᖱ匕⃦塑℃Ỷ⥎㣼灕掅ႛග䩜㕛〩埂ࡆ䡭㕝ᰃ᲍櫯䎧⹛ዠ㘗ं㚊恩怙⽚吥㡪ㄷ梏宊䧒硚⛐喭帒㓼䀿䆳㙆炠汈瑩津罃ᒳ㠬睜◮ᯊ㑔䞞❳♨஢崻稷璈᝴狏捾⛪䶗⧻Ô泪۳⅗㡭ƻ䵖檋䨾槒捠暼恎䄘匧䐊家⤂㎭离㑰漦⌉䧕熏⋸痓⪡᧌泘䣓⮆撦䎺୔ᴢ⳻᧋@朘✏椫ͧ琎念╆䓭䴼අ啀㳼ộ墈窷㔭氘㘸汱匣⸉௭盠潗溊曄仜㤳⛷䷗棡㚊ݏᔫ⢆䵨⟔灄婈⋳⧎䆖曷◛᭯堌楮䚫⇄ٍ去䃗冎⋾⛈க朘䶗戍ʎӾ唓➪७䋳ᑈ榋潷捀絯଑瘒ᨤ㐢歞垫₆敍♻Ṣ噭⚀旊䭦┯䋝榼㜨ء⽯䌆䧭㨭ዔ〦䫼㧌ᎇ⛨䕸尕ᘌ橎怃₆响䩱䫔溢䲀嗉⮌囵啕根㛔溹倭㫋㥍汉煔ⶎ墶ǓΞ㬌䵬檙㓺椻ᕓ⇶懍㹺楗涊┡⧚玚朗甕樅㗬橙宍㌶唅奊䙕从ࢆ㧕ʳ嬏ⶡ寣㘄‭宋ⵆ崨毹֢⥂㣳痀历㛏惹宋烹ⱀ帣⯦佭䢊ه窈勱䷞䉁㚸Y媩㓶濭坻⵲ຍ㓻䤢䥣樠竑占曎渚䅞㐱அ堅㠆杍羻ᥥ㖎国䊿孲⩄淳寡倮櫙嶃㍰ⶀ絻㧗⺎㠰爭㮇䛐㗸᫙㑮氉傓₆服嗺⛔ඈࡱ৑ж盓浫孢ᕊ汲ࡢᶖ瘴嵺นത㻳巁䵫团疧宙㝼榝倡㸖磭㿻૕疈㻷䵃宄朝皹檖咾⟥喛᝚䠍溺忖窊围㷚玄໲甿猀畡淝嵳⇌忍⭺㌷〃⋿䏄㎅囨洹⩮哦淩嚧⫆瑍佺㹄⾎ዺ⏉硙ຮ涡ᮌ㜤梭婕化䖒乛䇕璃晳懐絼䛝渃娩䔞澕凧㢠ᶭ湚䂗ដ䓱ෂކ䜦䢅᪀T毅怞ฮ媽຺◗塎僶Ꮗ捿ヴᷟ嬈療槳喧㢶檽䑓檖焉⧴矵孱㛇浗ᨺ‶殍屻⡮璉登⻵纊᧳乊㹼໗ᵮ㪻㖹槉吷⇖变㍺懔ᚋǷ૆ݴ折洠㮻♚毱崋ⷲ甽┺叔ᓂ᳻௒枒㚸嶏寠略潣彧₮嶥ᖻთᤎ೺揓㡟㓯ᶣ叜皮汓堼㣮择Ⳛ碗⬍೸䣃祩໮嶶孲ᑪ湝夳㾮不Ṛ䎔沉䧼৔㝪⻎䶉㯑㝠殕寧⩆瓽㧺⹔䜌泺㗕唣ᜐ崨冼矤槻前⽮䆅兛幔嬏秷Û㞃亦淣ն砍櫛寗⏖籭凛⇗ᮉ岭ᯕ⭱⋞ᖭ⩒瘢梅勗⦮毽㗻䪖ᆈ᷼珒㎈Ụᶓ㩕㔂沽孧◮䎽⳻垕猍׺珞睬慍嶙媎⏜漥埗ⵆ癝㡺ᒕ㼊函旗஛團丘簇圪泧垓㑟㌕䇛禖偵䋸秂垌༈嶬箉瘮桪ῇ┎䖍ྊ⚗嶊۱⟂஋Ầ㵔穞㛾澩宷Ⲏ恝⦚㎕喊䛽範侌ỳᴾ宅盽歩宷㈎涍䒛濲爉㛳埂ᥨ笑啟ᨬ皽渡ᬡ∘奝涛痖瘉ױ症㞗犬㵅㩡㕭䠵垑唶啽䙻哖֌Ᏽ᫟ⶆ囩ᷝ㫝疪樵号㏾棍智皔䈏巷௙᎝ᛋᴨ窍瘻欙岏⸚佝摛ᗕ嬋䏾߆ᾒἘ㴮箏㚲䗖巻⻺乥机䘔籁៻矏ඟ庸㶡笛㐩泴ࣛ⻾䖝෠嘔㮊۸◅瞖੮緄寋瘋⦮坿㾾扽䉻犗㌈⳱䗝䞐滩嵨字¼㜏囗⚞椝࿚箵਌䭰寔佲漞᷃筶睩毑奟㣎依憽兖᲎䯴㿂䊩纵ⵧ㮘㞶棯埯⭞䫝↼᠗岏ỵ⟐ᮑ纷緗嬗疑檇婿㝓ᒽ樛㊖耏矹ǜ➏䜁縃㬘瓯樷垿㰞壝Ლ嬔ઌ翶㿃殒Ǚ㶿㬝瘯棿峏⫾刣ܺ慗嘋恚৘੦䌇ฟ狋瓀ὀ㳿㴡欝䰧㑔ྈ䁝㧊䄌皠㷸⦸࿢桯岠憞擭㐦Ⱇ勋⿻⿛ĝ㼇㵕᫰ໍ樀㾠撡絝Ἒ䝕㠸篺ៗ䄕纱ᷗ篲畋渰㍀憆墣嘧搗ツ翼ߖ獩剆楦㏒᠟樯墀癠摝ⲻ⨬ᠸ㿾痃坭Ộ剶̍矸ὐ㖀⪞䓽奛ᘗᰈ⿷徕Ǟγ⪋疀ᨛ壗㈡抽⼦Ⱝ怈⧿描惼兇㷯婠瞋琏加耖猝┧ඖ不珰࿑䃢⇅ⵛ篔ໄᰏ忀竮扭゛皕唉[珌瞀⳷秺㪌瘇油兰揖耍ᠦ⤮ሿ䁐⟒惮月㵢ڒ෾毵嫰沞䭣性࠭㈉ۿႝ᭡⛙ᴡٙ㝕潗嚑㓢䍍㥛Э䘻史埔䨥だ穤Ƽ璌᣺⃮Ꮎ懩揚⨯有љ忁徆戝䎙箖ඌṢ墟⏶好㶚㝀Ḻ瑞嗘奰绻І嫨盵毯型Ⰱ䲰Ǜန压㟽炂ヮ䇦紴ڈတᯀッ⛡濩ⳛ̔∾௰䯍侘ᇥ洽尟晲㉔΀Ḥቭ歺搭۪打䒒僸盟ᵕݻ栂᳤㐄ࢱ川౧殢़枥࿖獥↴Ж޹๢ᰨた㺡䒽㺧ⲯ樾㡟⏉僽懩䷎މ㓓湤㉀昶竄ଧ沮昻ᯱὁ㄂ዘᵂ䝣瘨ቴ㶉ᙠ纣ے爮箉ࡕ咒ℑᇙ䐒䚯ᙊᴗ嗀橁䷭㵧䐮澏羻࢏羂ẗⵖ䜱఺᮴㪑㣱䞅籧㚭琌㩜ҎᄉǨͻ孺ഘᯱ8砡䯣֛䔖愸׿璕㮀懽緡䚃ಬᨴ㽧➎䓘渧䦯漈秽懋杨盬䎗篒ಜᴗ劸懁窃ᶛᆗ房瑟⟳棻⇅⵵䚅ങ楄㵰拾浣ᵻ洮欽ⷲ梉椒仵婴䝓拯槻ⴧ⹞嚽ុ嶯ㄽ癖䢞垊璬䐉篌ྒᡌ㉷⒑乃㻧ᠷସ⹖ᲈ僽懩㴵䃤ᬸᵦ很憶攀ⷧ⟦⍎໶Ở夁凷⏳櫫᠎ᱜ㋈磆畝Ϧᗫ䖌㿼㿋很ᇇ縞䂷က⦸㚘旱籅挺Υ嚉㹜䢌㾛爌ᐧ篫༪ᴬ㚸然惣濦䶖缹擹䯛ᾝ仸揺݀䲓沄ヶ∾琳宺ᄕ欿䅕䢝烼ሄፎ笳痖槛嚤擑䷝璚纬㞏䙑粕磮刅浻寧ආᢋ厸窑䧣㔦紬侈ㅜʎᣵ盵渀➈亥梋ᥨॱำㅇ宷券煜㢇儉憼͡篤䵂ẙ寈懄㊳〛/ʊ䯴ಃ愖䧢巩窧㜩檼㝄渁潣㧧儬栋⯽傎Ć廄推婔䳒ΐ处缩溃᧧怬ⲿ䏲犜ℓ䦪࠽箯癲ᴼ㮨梮珜䁆᠖ʾ剚犓䔜䨎Ꮎ❠䰲ᨌ㑳⤜ᡳ࿦ᅬ᤼橚䟀潹⇲ጥ竣๱潿僄絡䗃䳆䨗ହ敛促影曔叡➧ᙅ滊㴈炩禳扇¬ᚏ啗㟈ᮝ⨂䏻媐䱔䞛卄甑䄳㳦䑭⌸䩝巌㾄暻淭ݻྫྷ᪂ㅸ燞䍳⇆䵬䚽摐ᢑ᭡∉压ؽ౉▟䥠箉吜㳆ȯȽ䕜檋㔃繋喵㪸ญᤔኴ笪ຳ㟧䠖昋䅖犋䔄ㆫ嶓ᨾ䰹ᯯ弴滩禃疻井纸ᵝҟ㮌熳向嫞乜⌊ㄿ⟾厳䑺僭耗畒㟚ᓹ䧢卜䠌痣ἤ楤瘹寝⟦瘯䨹姾⯇㉣㭚䎩ᬊ痑᲼㭄瞖䈳坺朮䚻⧽毕⣢㻚㏗媣㚊䥠㋬絴味卆޷຾ⵖҕ䳨ৃ䶺叱൅涯垨悆耙䟆࣭吊獝෇䳻槫叶⟭౫ᴚ㱌灑桃᭧↮㦼単檅ഇ䦭㌸⚉ಔᳺ㒋⽶孳؛翕媺歙緝攋⻰㍍䚵㙻ᾌ㻰珉䜃㒺曮䄿䓹㚉瓲ᨎ㏏❍瑒沖㷀珹嵃䓇ᩮҽ╒ຈᔓ仾᎔㭷࿥ౘ㎟㭹拳嶆盭梿ݛຎ⤴㧛㵑昲䵧ᣪ㡳⍮壃啇≬䨿繻参㤂沪㏶晾䲣Ḇ㯨煆皎獧痭䮼慛㺩棬ᦣЍ曍䵁槖㺗㿹柝㛧ᣮ㮹穑悍├ມ掂曧䴁氦㐰殱䞳唆◯䞻ᕛ㧇ݧ㛲⡶Ѱ࿏ᣰ⒀䆉澓㉧ବᰈ潖Ή㴑倽王暭䷺ᩆヿ㘩哓㋺䧭瞺㙞⒚紆姵嵥笳ౡΐ弌皉擭⾇㟭ᶊ塓⺞㳽㧯玱杂䴙ᱥ匌糑囐ᐧ偏㮺䏼䚎ⴟ㨋䷐᝶疋ض㆐箁滳ష䁷㶹䭘埏洓㇫司ᙴ俧橁㟐箁纓ɛ׮স䔄࿊䌎秠௖枠⺱῁㿨斥忣巽癬檊噓檕ࣲ⩼గ朸⸗᱁㊯⾥䤫⇧⍮㴺畝揗䌔懟珉㨠⳥ᡁ㔜牥嫳✆⡮压屚┫紆京അ箓乥ᠱ㵼楥涓禇珖οᩝ冔̚⧎ଭ㎾皢ῐ㟴拙窙⬆㷭ѿ潒㒌㴟漕௄❆仛ᡉ嫢憞濣᫚㍔枼牓Ҕ拲ש䍯٘⹗ᬯ堯㺥棣☆⠮縸⇷Ƒ⋢؅ଧ昲⺁毗媲沶傝⚆ᷬ᫪ᓞ䦛儆◨䭂ឪ临濆㞘沙卓紆睯㾿凹ᚙ指⊳Ꭲᙬⴠ孑㵲煹籫䘆㽬䒿䏴榗⌘٘᷍ᛩ乷ᠺ㴔毅匫ặፕ穸㍚᪐㌔䈘㷯ޘ⽜ᭉ㬐矹敫ᔷ≎㙿Ó⧁焞㦹ମ᠈痨安㔉㗥簫ᶷ嵍≾哜墈㳻曭అ䟩矊᪐㐲漾篫⏦䜔似⍗䆂ᤎ昌䯱ᘼസᨘ㘒橱宣⸶綗ⱨ泑憁䌌昁஛ᛶ⿢宁㒒縵箣⠦癔瑺᝚→攖ᘋ఑柏┼ᴉㅲ漅啫㠦ᙏ穼⿰▎ᴓᨑ二昹ⶌ弬ぴ焥啫偆彯䚒ⓘ犓狡⚷፦᛼⹂夑㼈窾瞳℆楔㒼拝Ɨ⓪眆们堒丨᥮㯬晙氣穇⏮ូㅚᦘ䞇延ᐛ殬佼壩㮒溅緫笧礬籽峼ን㋰弎叀䟍ⵘ岹㌂窅俓妆奎㱿㏱秌㔊滛⬻㫄ೋ澩姊眵䒫ၷ㫎妏櫔疀ଋᗷ⭂圡疺廅䀊綑禃耒ᯬ᠊⛝府惜䗹嶦噽ⴢ宕ㄑ㉺⨓ؙ⮖卸ᛖຖ⬍槯午ړ䱬寵㶸籕楋⍶䣏ź䱵巑㋽☆Ꮛ婶ⳕὍ㶳ᜊ⭓ؚ䇖挏઺礡ૹᘃⰌ嚒琹ᨽ㵊㖎䄋䧶䋭渾穙㺖䌘娙厁ᝠາᲞ㓺熕埃秇柬䙼ۗ冁徕㗰毕堞⿶廭㹪礵楈囷䥭ཹ⭗㢞ᓺ姹厯坕䰪姙㆚沕牋៶۬䂾ῳ勭爌受ᨿྎ᤽ヺ硵嘃侚₌ㆿ᫐歚ܕ᎗ⷍ窷⹘摣㫚繵懳㨇῍᭺⇕㢗㫽戋⬡嚈ⳁ庑偦砩尋⳷硌獾䛞疜இ爊վ垟痱塉㾌犴㎽៺悌㽼㛛䶝䛽弖᭩ᙌ瓄孩偆紭偓〦墎獿䓼ᎅメ㧦⌭ሀ洡害㠦涕啣禦溮⃾Ⳕ厜㔝伙᭩ᚘⲛᯧ嗼粭祫灗ᯌ⓸᧒ẜ૴懮振垯矸庝㮆柵䜻䩗៍᭿䕝熚䫻䷧ᰙ暑ⴱ川㙜砙旫孊痏౽໕掚䜕◊⭫᜷习娹䀛㭱囋僆ⲏ樔⡘ஔ実稃ᮼ㙀澬ㅖ㲶罱漻皦稭渾翽຋⓳䷠⭎㞓⼵廮㩶紙姳ᶦ坭䫼䛕⎝✜盚孍稺瀑忦㤐曅捻䕶泏ᅼ䧕殏ደ䷎嬽嫨瑒ᥠ㹖梵枱䔆↌䳸⩞ஊ㛾㻅宠ӲᇠѨ΃ᎌ、㞌ᮠ㛺㪵宄✌禨䬵㜏㢦ͻ㟖狠ǻ㝢㮏囼淔ા≀㶌䃷壖濡ᏼپ਍堀ϖ䚏㙼旚㎔盻淧寯㟤䐣宠Ȗ碠⛸榘ྎ䇾廭嬷硨᷐㯐眮澤带㊖撳ր⢖एǸ揓ޞ眛淉ᇏ㟑泅⼛㋪濍咋㒗焏㒫㨱➄喒㨾█槺ጹ឴彮摷㊻ۧ⪎⼼ႇ➜ണᶪ♬矙沪睱涿Ỵ捛↖භ৸⫔㪌伇ᷞ㬭䪌㪫希岡ࡽ枀㐙䓘戲≅枙⻻ዔQұ濎岌ブ拧Ὓ䶗⬎橸䛤㞍Ჩ嶺沜矰ЅԶ㈴殽䷛擛挌ヾᷞᎎ箣帚⋩㬅漒ⲍᮎ櫽僛䐁Ⅷ嗾寞੕伙營揑娣[崯㺆婝䮱䆖㼌ἓᆴË仲㸔ഹ堅瑫峣㘶烽僛㔗҇溵⟒ᄯ˛೰䡼矕燪滱柮拝嘝哗崔⍽Ꮬ殚⻰嶺篏簁⮷嵮Ⰺ殽犛ӗ帏叻埒▎㜏涣㯭皝滑䱷⟾犏ⱆ↗㩚⮪埓ᾆ㡜没篓㜥⺥嫫㍮䮽洛實朌៺㫭⓻建ᘱ㮃眯涧嫆㸛⓮䈛䡹搚⿾䞠侖甹ຯ෡皥江崺卺綩灻嘗玍哽࿟㾕䝡Ʃ箜癿漁捩䎖搞ࠧ㗗㶎◺㟘灜Ǻ䗢囐໶೾הڱᯐɈ怜兙侰ₚ䄕䉇倬ߚ癴洺ᤇ㌡礣绰㐯㠽䲊㯤䄇㜖Дޔࢳࢰ㿚֒Ǭ媁Ⱞ禡ᡜ䀿䄍企Ϝළ䍸ṿ䪓ᅏણ䨧㘮亅䅃炑⍌ǣϴݝ㶽溩壽㉞碣甧㘯搏溲࢚℔引檑݊Ӈ䪩Ӡ畁涣皧〵厍㶮⡞㶙曻巾ࠚཏ昸㯡⒴碮ᚧത㨽ጮ丫擁両䣷ޮ涄ᴽ奧ㆁ绨农㬯䄰屚᭤䱕݋愉ᆥ䖼዇乿㪁條禧ᴖ夘≝氻ّሊ狊䤙墓ǳ䡫㺱緑ڛధ帽䓿䒓❻ᇬ瓥㫥มຎ柞䴁ۉ橡યᯣ⊬炞ྑӬۺ䞹␢Ᲊ䆈畱竦ЌՈ噗Ȅ滣㗒Ȗ㸕篕瘚ἔ㢷䩑狆䖜ᄰ勻Ⰶ䲛Ϋ戒ᶢ䟣ཁ䗬㮈纕ᖃ滲栵磳Ჳ⃹ᒰ㈋巢䟕疖ᾌ㽓ⲑ斲૕Ո㎠瞅ݽ廊爁䧎㶣睟漯弟㋵✚巧氋兵⋒๨矅㵱⫪ℜ櫗埍〘翑柣懧红缼⢿嵈᫘৥掾¯悎⏳冉摵⸳糰慸෪俹歟殊檀檴✨俱ᶻ⽺宩洳宒溋兵澡⏀䮐㖙Ꮀ❫༞沲㋄義揚淍܄᜿揫⯐ᛇ䶎❲㎏矩䲟徝㜱禃凕砝焫姊哵攋嶌窈㡨俶噪㧄罁昃涚䇋㊾䕘᭣:๋ᐁ 佉ḫ⳴睉罽䋇灮㳶留⪞Ѧ䔌䅂喤垁ⓔ熩祙噇ᅝʹ浘ኝ૒槥搁磨櫍᳴䃦埉綽伧䈭ͷ嵙፲唐ᨅ㫻䞛睎ዽ⛁㋶ㄾ⬕䘖ᜰ崤䚓甛䇰䛷䞿༃ᱦ㣺ሑ柞窇ӯᦾ慞瀯ԓ樎Ꮔ朷䜝Ệ㻢䱹敳熇塮Ṣ劷撁攚ᖄぜ悕仏⓭妨甑恳嵇罯䢾歞⹎㪛ᶁ᏾枛ᡎᱷ䬏淉朚婤楲ଽ痽窒䴑⨖竩杹倐琏̎叾愕䦨秋縌ᵿ㓐㖃ᜇ㎥ࠓ俶哈㢂ᑵ⍣秇痋栢ϲ刯ℷ桞ŭ喤㯉祲㱶䧈ᓐ᨜煠瞼ໍ媐纀稁叒⟯俏ᷞ㤜翹栺䘇翯⾾潝嵹櫇娓㏞朦楫͓渓㲽⋓儇溹憪Ԏ溕㦏䧥ฒ寞࿫ᵶ⦢等ห窬◮䶾津䆖䌐ᵱ⫦磲例嘴䌜缂毓帷橏亾溼ᒡ㤎疠碝傾乘忒ᇨ紱揅汧ᱎ悽ՙ熕挅⨈䮮షည碖ۈ羍㠺姲棄▼⏹凱⛏畢䯕䠅਄峩㬎夠ኅ༃ⴊ⁼嵚曣禅὿昉㎆຤帪㶎嶉磫眛⑏拪泚睵礄ॎ岦柹俣᱆㩲瓱架沇ཎ弌់⚗猇爊昘叞涒㬃䒅㆟ⱋ毨࣎ഽ俹⇷ઘ羔⮺㚼囂嵘প煏ⵆ溷ᴙʌ઎斒㌈攉瘓អ⺺滃廫㵯㽋嶷ெ⃎⫟勑㿚䨄⮯挭⼂庂㪷㢹䜉捍看娯抾功予䨂Ꮹጭሚ怂㺼灡瓓崇G἗ۚ疛Έ㗡㏴⠔瘓伢㹉㻄焎缷差㾏睘᪑⃉┄ᐊⰖځ‘姙ਔ䘄潋揎⸲忹Ở羌竩⯦箅⿺屵㣚禆紋猲Ⓐ呏䇇▒䬗ᗬ▰䭬㡞尵匚狵滳孷◍Ἦ绘䐯笜ᘓ殦ᶟ⾲弃䠒㸴磳羋Ç䚽Ǟ纝嬎ᮛ槤㜸Ė嵥安檴睳杻ᗯ彿᝚樥猚䴂䨊㷃俁彳㿮㜭栭䍹窏瑽ռ㆚ܓ潳ᯍᯄ⠉徙女埀⻽浳供䵕租᎞㾓攝䇁㟴Ъ嗖墫㯭牻治劎掿坞櫛⚑㨓ᯕ篌潆峋㹆秭曆浗嬶䍼僘㺞勈ᾉஶ杂渲屏ỉ㪍濓猓ۓ囿ݚᶐ䔩พ䶢䷆俭庇泖稌画璻㞎潼㡼䎑䬄䷡ຠ瞠潦嶐㼺耘枋畝愎᳿⓹䞙笞෭丐卸ģ榢倆粍欻橳ᔏ獣⮃⮕羈䇻ᰗ緩漖෇㵪疽擛疌⻇㕼㮾⽈猏ḓ探瞺潤⽷㧶筽潫殓ݏ淼囜瞓䬍෣ி東滧䳗㱙ヶ㛋摓ぎ㞿彜䆐厑婵琐ᝳ瀏Ί㿟妍犆昇៯ᏽÞ⽟䣎㷦簉睽➵ἐ年矽斻䄗䲏⍭࿜᳐椶⧢ᮯ援漺崗浶粝絻樗浺䗾濜㾓ᶘ罾宯獌៴屓㦉堝绛囷䜏Ͼើ䦘匍ଞໟ睽⟊䲧㢪篢瘧䝗ㄏ഼⧚ᕓ纐䫼ߍ眦លྒྷ㲖祹洋䄑秏᝿༻ۓ㬃娅䮭㟀ṝ㙶㬿弳㫓瑋从㏿᫞℟ଃ渓ֺ䷭⽏幐窵㫛⼛䳋ⷺ矽῟枖ⴐ帛㘗矺渤䶶塶睵搑焒ᦩ獣纺▞䞃⡑߿䯄ᾪ徰絊箥瑧繗汈牜咛ភ则⏢䟎卬澘ⵀ編筠罃糇ှ柾䑽䞔ẁ剎޿睕ᩅ崋獙ㄢ登嗞ᘿ⵿⁙椞䈈㎐寔⬭ჼ㰶扩㨳絛忁Ć幟ာ夕Қ搞叻࿏湡Ɽ约窳罙弯༾䲮Ῑ礜܏揳㰊䮢ṧ役楼璲愛䯗᮰䟾犟⎔䨋វ⚫砂嘪㝿㿶甍朻耗嚾歼ペז∟䧥޷砍㰈痛㲡爳炻䭯㘎|⃜⾝漜㐜篭睠Ἒ㲃㹩絲暇漗⦾㫼㫨侘̏㸃尅圤ᾶ崨碎牃惇籭綿劎ໝ結અẌ⑷櫨濢䵼絕体歧炷㬿㩜ᅧ崙喰揻柒禶夐㴰繄緶窋北糧ỽ劌̜ᮀ厀៎叮〃ộ㺉㺇❓叛㢾Წ杞⚙༅球↤⽲漜溨庥焹繻縯Ⲿ獾ଡ଼㴗㬛⏡⟩䵔Ộ㿰禑瞍梧筯ᨿ啟篜ⴐᨔ䔅ះ䭤幬㹛㭑煳猧䥏⠯睼璟䓰爜棰垤眽湮彌汢絵竅䓏ⁿ䍯晿击ᘘ㐘奇埾㚏ư䞉秸ቤᔇ⑿㊮粘ଞ☐㐚堉氌庽徊羶缕箷屏瑷惾禘ᴜȈ珵ެᷖ徥䀍㿓妋汷䙯䱿浞熜禗昈㈅ࠔ⼢䟝㽊縕瑷⚷䱋皻㳞ۙ䎑܂搚毌ល丶㻴祂㋜癅巏抿㇞ゟԜ㘛囶垭〞帮ᵹ㩹瘍糷硏᮱租΀ㄔ嘗䋲堛⿩弽㴦籥坻殧泏⻆惞硻̟⸉琑㞶⽕᫛㵲簙磕憧緗端囜ෘᆒ⦱䯩簆⿉幇㶱㹙䫽缫䌏∨硞ෘ̞帐專᏾澐笈㺎緁稫綗剫ᖾ孝⚘ᄒ㸒㐇琎濄徾㲶筩军憛嘏楖࿞㟜僟眊毢ⷼ㐌ឞ巺纽紝皗䫝笧燼ǝ䖙丘ߴᰜ猭⺃㽐緵琘罷奏❿璖㢝ᬛ欁䏰枤࿈漟㼨確碧戥矗䜾ᵞ㋘ᓵЇ䯬ྤ潝ῐ崖簭瞛碯捇䚾㝂儝㳛痐ϡࠐ࿦࿞㒈縉畧翇漏晟婿䮚滭ȁ䐎柢⾛䥚㴒㪹ㅧ楗眿^応檍ᴐ␜珰旨ᵌ㽤緑箵瓔慷才畟䅞Ԟ榓ȗᯭ㯓⼥忏䀒硣瓻痧憿◿ᗜ⶟㼖ᘈ栘࿠矆㸣㴑簣缋滯䠿ⰿຜ募燒฀䏸㠛䜩査ᶑ秝珛濵傻ჾߜઈؔ␂實ޯ潪漲渣污羇积冏橞畝嶿䘚䰇渖⿯’柪㽺碋ᕳ瘯想ᪿෝ᚟塐樖㘊吕➆㸝彔滏䃷敮䚿╶⯧ᬚ೻ك堖⠢Ƌ欆㣝⛳⑷䖠罿らጊ䬙䳟縅ᰝĒǻᰦ籷咳汗皏棿彅೩䔇Ἇϩᡚ濔忻幒绑҃䗗熽㻿监尉㎆ျ䳥戠砪ņฤ庈紫篗溄◿☢烀⼜㶂㰞枴㎳Φⶼᯮ狽筩痯宦ⷽ暈Ȝ烚स∧᱌㼬宏䁋▗掯帓寎暞澘⒮ࠃῃ䤈㼰翁篵盶呗絺悬⇩ᎠᏱ䧉ਡᒙ⾼ᾓ⋑繻ⱓ慯撳桨⩕拫䐗䗷Ԯ俬垜㾤縺櫩兇瓫檏獟⟟緀稛㠃緤㠄➲Ƣ纶縹ᶇ珸ᕥ❟᧾厞䘝㍣㪩㕬ྙ㿟⡾樤⥷缧䵿磟Ⳕ洝☚㐉ᰂ埿᝿࠾秵絣㓷笢䔥ǔநࡿ⍜濧ũΑ௜㿺罅绶嚷翏沿綨㮞圝⩅惏䅼曇怂ᝍ畿䥛㴚⛢᤭浘㠵ᶠ䐘嘪⊢⿱ 娵絩緂礗熏牟皊椞監侳Ê䭥 ᥔ耎ȧ䯬ᗯ稿砾Ɵ唟䘞Ḙᐜ砃俾怌Ὡ缒⊷穏线琼⧒䔅✹䮳᠝န岩ќ务於䠷祙殹⇒ⲟ皟䔜氜ᴞ砞忹㤡羭擉⭮㊿砼岴 ߶穘༾穐穉㩖⚤積㩃㩇䱋㩕儩穁皩穜䨡穙撠ٙ䬩欨穐牍穌穃穄䘷䱚愨ٛ⪡穟穜ᩈŶ穊ᩏ檹昿栢⦲娧㌧㖵搯⚤,䨦亹ٜ㾰䙀༪㜾伨ſ眴䙔䔭َ#ّ簫و洷ٖ⠫尸㠠怲צቊ琹䒲穃ਢ䙜传ʪ濺怫ܧ䙆伩ᜲ䙙撿眤♕伤犺䙖䙎>䙇ٖ⺩䙊株%䙍䙘⩔㡥౏婖⺼♔♜暻♗伴ሿ眪‴♉ࢰ晇♟̺♏቎♊1䙈䠡㉟ᠬ琵⊹♆5䙞秽䙝♀剔伨晗䙜粿䙂щ伫晆伱း晛憿眨ᙒ♕ك璦䙒晐疾♎䰱♓桗⡄⠥⊶媩晅晋㕭晈㡣晛䙌ᙞว晚傯晐伧ᙍ⺭䴸栬翳石㼴䲤噕⏴(㱏⺠溿檥੖庴溥㰢溰溰㰫䪬䀳䢳ㄥ䂡溬ᨹ溿㶭溿抰䲪噈䠩⑀噝梢䤣4噂ᑢ䤾Ἥ㢸㙞Ἳ㱗⺭⠾噊溩ኮᙎ┼䐫噒溨溣␦享噜䐧噚῭㨿噔網䩃ਲ噑㙌㙗溡㙟歡碢䤸䀻ᚼ抸㙑癚噙᡹㙔溧㙐㰡С♓㙏恕噁噚溡♖溼ⰾ溸癑恔癛ᠼ癜渥癉癕吻溼㙜傶๗櫲噄堿◱俢㙁ਲ硊᱇㱅㙛栭㙇癃㙌溻㙍噒ⰿ㙄่癑溲๐㙃溢䤭๔㙁ๆ癎乛ๆ攭㧲扇䴦⇤状噍⠭塠也㙁㸫㙀ํ㙃噕䐠癎溠硪乍垪๜㡜'垺癛㒬秶⹘㙊㙌噗㣽ᶲ噅⹇ใ癗乗㙐乀ᠶ⠠⹟癟๗㙄⹜溻噌๒⹅溺⹂㪣⹚㙞๞䑁⹙⹚㙕乖癑籑༬2癞扫乗เ湘湛癟乘么⹄湜乜湂⹏噊⹆乕儣湕湁乁湇ⶳ湞಺ṁ癎้඲噕癋⹃媷湋癊㐯⹓噐湌湛ṝ␴湌⹔์Ṅ療Ṛ圦湙๖ṙ⑞Ṛ幅湙九๐㣪䬵๛๛⺧湇⹟湉噟Ṅ乐๏㙉噂乂湜Ṋ湒Ṗᘩṋ์ⰾ⹎幑幆㙃短⹑䒴䲼峡夻乓癔乑噄溮┯恔≍㹈๎ᙚ呀幇㹑7੓噐㹌幂โ幚ไ傰䲥悪㹎ၺ繖㹄㙘呬\"ෳ⹝幃癕㙗⹟㙓㹍⠻㹏幘幟㹗幍㙘織⹔繗噜幄㹒幖久繎湌і幎繙繄㙍⺢෮㙛憱㹊㈣ṛ栵㹏幗Ṕ⹛繖⠷繘⹟㙀ňṐ㰸Ō湐癈㹜ŀ㙒ŕ儭Ŋ癑乂嬮䅎癔喺繝紥ṕŕ䅝ṍ繓ṃ繋幃㹓ㄿŏ湌义噘䅈ⅇ੄Ṃ䅌繍⠺乆䅛窳䅎๖ő็刭ŝṉł㹙癁Ş乛䅓ŗ䅇ṋ繀⅀䅘Ṅ⅐Ṍⅅ吠㹔ṌŜ繂Œ繑娭ŋ⅑ⅉ乂෾乙渦⤥;⑚侾∵態㉂尧湗⅝㹗癄慐幗㹟⹔Ŝๆ⹓慍䂱⸶繍呤Ȳᅜ濶ᅍ慍庢ᅑᅛ⅍栫ŏ义噏癀繏繂⅜⹒慆⹟⠡ᅊᅁ䅓㺨兜濫⺫粳乏檥㹏慘溠ᅅ噔慟幆溢慌ᅉ嚮⹄兏濱⹅粲㙎湒光湍癆兑兇ŏแ先ᅉ兘ๅ兎砠兖湆琺ᅑ⺻兑Ņ㱁ṉᅆṕᅎ噈ㅟ⅔ㅐ繘幔ᅊㅍ兕ㅁ慂ʹㅐΌṕ⹀旣嚭ṁ⅟̰ㅌㅘㅙ噐⹑兇ㅒㅌ␿ㅔ煆幉⅁梲煗櫡ㅋ⅏兆㹍ㅏ๖煓ㅁ煌ㅉ煒⅟ᅕ煝⅞湎ő产煅义ㅘ㙐ẫ⧱១ㅉृōᅖ兝㙟⹋ᅐň慙兜ॕ党愵॔渺ृ煀ሸ䥌槶琭也⡉悪兙㹗慃ㅓᅐᅛㅗᅔ幂ग़愮᮳溮ㅒ偱⹙ᅒ⠼抨光㹒Ԧ煐繎煏Ő慝噈䅙䥏幌䅄幒久煅ᄰ⥝煗溩⥘噆㑞㙂䤽㑚煁䥈ॉ䥋㙊⡔य़㙊⡋ㅆ⥕䥞⥊䅌癜ᅘ㙝㑛䥟喺楞ಯ䥃漭湂噈光楝ढ़ㅗ⥟䅟⥉੐䅉噘楄ॐ繖⥗ㅘ㹚䅆慅ε楆楃兆ᅋ慍楊ᮾ楖᮲噋⥛湝繑䥋楏恀楅䥏楝縠ᥔ楜慀䥏ㅃ䥑᥏尶楜ᕨ奆㙆刧汑៲癐㿸⥇⥔⥓ㅏ恕堰楉噘ଧ᥈Ō楒䅑恒᱊楖㙄ฤ奍Ἲ奄抵楏汍㢸㥆奂縤⥛Ł奚⅑煟㙕奈湌ㅈᥙ煍㨻奟抬㥙⥑䅝㥎ᥗ奁᥁㙜㥇慅ᥓ楞兑奖㥅奚⥝奏᥏ᅜํ⠵㥐奏㥃㥂⼳䥇㥈ڣ8瑈Ţڵ祝楐फ़奏⥍奏ूㅟ᥄ᥒ楉♝㿦牄ㅐ暸‿ି奖丣祋䵾撶Ս庡Հढ़ᅓ繗祁㥓ᥟॊ祊ㅄ՗⡌ՙ噈䥉Ր煀䊡Ն攩Չධ䕛⥛⹕᥁♇幄䅘⅓Ս䥚祉溢繕⠿䚯Ձ㸯弰䕚Ն咤䕙ᴶՎ㹜煟娿䕋祅Տ䅘祇織祄溴⅑㥃奊⅙䕚慕䕔Ղ㸳噛繖ᘸ╔䥋ܸ╘噍ॉ繉澤䥉㙇䅚䕈乄楗楁䕜楊慔ᥑ奋Ⱗ奏╘セ䕟梢䤭ु幖敒㼲噇╀敓œ幏⅛幜祟祎ᙘ᥂楊๊敌㠦⹜㹝敞敀ᔭ敔游噖г璼㱨ŭṇḡ楺兎奊㥏⥏恖ᕌ㰦╉噓ᕐ᢯祔䅖╒慍⠳ᐵܹ᝺ἡ季戬ᥒ縡癉ᕁ神ņ̮ᕈ㥆ᥗᕀ⥙啖啙Փौ⥀ⅅ啛ᕄ溥啄敗㙉㥐Ս㨤啟䐬嬼啘⬥Ȫ啑楅啃╓㥍啑啍ⅇ╃⥂෽敒䕐效祘敋㹒╁♚═ᥐ啉䕆ⅈ䠩溺效㙁Ŝᕊ᥋ᆵ䅉敜ܳⱣ缮畃啈敟⹎䒱丿ᕞ䕘๘抸㕑恋⒤暯䬫䬦⹚䨥嬬攥䜮畚⼮戵洩䡻憽ᔢ൙ᕞ䥐祇祏啔叭畈幜乐䩑䕑溥畊啚ൎ⡒ᢦ籊仼േ൑ℯ慯嚸䵟汛慺澸䵜䨽䀠 ࢺ䵇䂤.䵂⼮䵅᲻ࣺ濼噑䒰⩝ײԳ䵌㚹㊬穙愲䠴䱇ṋ㴧䵊撴ⵛ㺴ⵙ撲㠲ⵙ䬧䵗䪿䵊䠨ⵙడ䁆ⵛ⪺ⵕ䵜幻㸽⤻᪭䵞㹅۫ⵎ皲儴䔮ⵃ㪡ⵐⵕՖ䈦縩ⵏ搡缠浙愨流皫縰浍ヲ堰⩏凰栭浐⌤浌嚬浚浚㐸㿰ᩏስ浛࣮塏䐫ܸᵞ屙ᴢᵖ◤䁺ᵘ浃ⵞⵕ㘠ⵏ浗砠ᵓ♃ਮᵉ♞塜ᵃ浛ࣩᡳ测垤ᵋ流ᵔ浉ᵑⵕՍᵛᩚ愳浘лᵂ嬭浅䵍䌪㡯ᵞᵈ⩑ᵙᵂ嵉濫ᙞ戰⩋ส.嵈岥嵓㸦塢漤㵘嵍嵔嵃嵋幒嵋穎漬㵖嵌ᵅ⑄㵘㵞䠦ᵟ罦塿ѻ浏䵌嵜浚㵋嵋䙇焣㵔ᵑ嬩㵕㵚挾Ĭ㵉ࢶㆾ㵟̫㵛桧㵅ᵗ㐿㵐ᵓ墢絉Ŀ嵑㵜㇭絜結㡭㵑༺経絜㵃㠽嵜嵏㵒忻嵈ᵍ絏嵀㵜暠͂⁌〯凡͈͗䵞絊㵛敆㵋㴫摁㵄絜㇡̓㬬〯絓㼧࠳㵄嵇流絓嵜̀絈ᵀ䍘絁塗͏䀿ᵛࣱ⬧孡ᛰ⩙䍐㭮絑᡼䍌͇⿽ᵇ嵉䍏渣絇͜暭䍐樴炽䍏炢⍙̈́͗㵝͙絏䍏ሣ株⍛͎䍂塢啞碢⪡孾ቭᡫ⍔⹶ⵔ䍛㵍͑噃͇ゥ⹡⏫ᵓ絍⍌捗櫩⍉ᦴڡᛶ捛䱚⍒㵔͎⍒䍅絃ࢿܦⱂ捘⍑亱捆ⱄⲲ砠╃ไ䂾㸨⥂縦㵑䵵⊬簧䵄᪢͒⡈ፖ䍎㡌ፋ凤䥊絟ᐼ⟢፞⍖⚦灆ፃⵎፊ䍓墣ፉፏ䡘卝ᚥ䴦౷ᚢ卐㭲ፅ歺ፗᵈ⩀千损尺华啖॒∯瑼千瑢⇪卛华䥒Զ南ፁ千㠩十⍑娹嚯卋䥒畈᱃卖ᐢ⇮悶ࢹ≑㍃敏摙ᨶ牓᭨䠤摘摏͋㴯㐭䒱ɞય㍗㒠ⵇ䚤獖Ⴐ䵁皰䵈ᢠⵅႬᢦ獟䩌㪰暾獊撧ൗႹᴦ岶⠶䈽瑈簳獓娻⒢岷獈渻⪣獋獄ጨ簠㱧⁃⁆⁈Ŧ岢୓᭪ୋ湞沯ሶ୊牁歨⍕⍑亥୒ଡ଼㉗ឿ樵漨ᒨŴ噂ᨲ卯獟沨䭉樫獁皼䭄䭊∤知S娸䲵戲䭋梬樹䭍ⵉ䭀稪ᵑ䠶秡䭖⁛䭝秴䭜䲨ᵟ䭍䭓⡟娯㠳璠⭖䭑䲿䈩R䭉බ⭐୞咱⭔⭀獘⦥⭓䭖㒱⭌碲㼻⭚碫梾ᰩG⭁皰歖⢽恵୆␴㪹撢歒怪歋梦歎歛⪡歃⍓炰୊⁁⁇⍍歗⁑୊剆䢮ウ歑䊿歛ୖ犹璮ゥ愩⭘箭䌶⠼᭙䭟沯䌺ᭆ栢᭍籞ᭆ᭓⭃ⅼ⠮ジ歎䆣ᭌ歈沧᭘歍籚塳ᭈ⢸㵘孃⒥兿᭖天塡缲孚⒰孖孄⒨Ľ氷䭟嵹孜ᒨ⭑娽瞵⭚≅灭孞≅礹≀㭜墥≊撥翷ܲ䉞ᕁ捂㭓ᢺ㭖䉚㭓㖩幚喬ľ䵙㭊g培ᴺ欹ᶸ綿栩᥉େ尧⸫㭂⼳㭘楏䕔場䉻憼ᢪᇷ歀ᠲ筜⋧制筋䒱᭜交碩筚翡夾⪸䵚㐯ፑ卓筙卌環忶၌⭐䒵筅㟴ሿ扔牘੘༼ݚ䩞䩋祃ぺィ枲堡ݍᐲ㠼ᠿ⸵䐢ᨭݛᥚ愺ݒ݁皷݅䩁⨦挦݀ਖ਼撷း䝏݅㍔>ݍࢪ汴๾⵳ݎ梣ݕݎ械癓䐵搾ြ扉倽堡䁬⩖㵀瘼䝉橤䝈䁍⭍ἰ❙䩖݌ୋ㬩ݛࢳ⒢岺❞䝓ፀ祃媦ຯ渭⤱䡤堬՝❀ᢼ⩷㪺ધ堿ክ漧ᒾ❆䝞ⵧ‱䀫ܶ୔杒䥗㸻ဦ❜ギ䆳⠮村❋祕❒ᔼ䪺恅⸲摖杞杘ギ䩍牜沩杗杖瘼杆佣❒㭑៴᝛❊ᑟ̤捕優ᝐ堼ᝈ䠼杋ܡᝂ娾⡏Ⴎ㍃搴䜦怬㢹癋ᝏ⊹࠯ᝄ猪㕙㤢杊楀坞Ĩ坁㢤✬➹䜢⼡栲均ᝏᝊ❈⵻獝羶撠┴块崼坘杜୍坖㘼坟瑞❍坑[䝓坔㖳⠼㝈撤坖и崢䩆⹗㸺㝋฿杁䩐ᝒ怹㝖瘼䝊ᴬ᱘ᄻ㝉浿沿㝄唻⪨睝恩㘷售栱焹撼睌㢪睋梦睁㢮睛⪡睒睔द⭌缻⻬煄ፊ䬭Ჳ睙⭃睌።ᕇ䴷睄䡑恘ᠮ凹称ぜནᒲཉࡍ䪳筗砻筄㍗筅ᙛ&㠰Ẽ∸᭕琺䭃䕕儶⠺ཊ⌢ạ皿ག焦ཙ庹ᴶ⠹氹ぐお佛偍癃筕劧報མ㍉౅བ⚵溽ཕȰ栥樽歛ཏ୛⊲佐⭴罭籐⽕汝ᚮ⨪䭡簷㝃☨梲⽞⤰㭩ཕ佑佖桙抪檨⚾箹孋⹼為䄬嬮ᝃ᱐⭮⽛䉘砵搰潇孍ἶ⽞簾⽋䒤⤤忦潋塅佔㍖⚡佐ⱨ繘᪯慽⽓䢥⸩絝捌㍙∷甦ኢ㔱⺿潚➳岹楂翱㯿沴ὔ㭁淴ሦ簹筛憮Ὅ筀㍛፟䝃਱ὐݔ❖丽ὗ櫨孓潙⽞塳᭔䵘مὊ栬簯຤䉔帰栧㘵搦栦牙南὜䵎_᭒䵖仸撬Һ⡆嬱䠣杍塋彋潞暸案㚴桅䀫㴢ᠷ彟婱䠯␬䥚撬㽊滢㽜筅ỵᬱ㥺ڽ㿤桌嚾Ф㽑㽕Ṯ㽇ặ任㽟存䀴㽉ٽ义俥≐罄Kၕὒ悴网油Ļ㽊㽅翬网I⒱杒怫⒪ቈ橏橏ቜ᪾ੇ栱੏㉛則网坔牁ḷⰶ桁核牐㉘㉝暾当⠫⒬⢵居⑖Í⒧牓ɐ੕Ð⌽ᩄ橛罛䘢⩟罀牐Ö瑘Ü⠴Ð牜ß剒Ü牚×潛㴶歎孎S⠵ÑVᐽ慝╳⠹䃐䉊੃ᩖ੅氧Ï罊⩟Û䘨Á⸤䃕⊬䃄牌牞玦Ò怽䃙屃䢡Þ᡺⃗ᵩ䃃ᵠ䭍Q⃜⠽孋ቓ䃋Ë搧罗ß䃗吠䃖ᐸ⃏䝗剜䃔牊Ü㚪⃙䃈渾Þ剑Ý⃚⭕唩彨溲㝎⤿ᰣÛ⃟橛Ô䘿⃜੐惐⃐䃄惌ÁḼ惂⃂牊嵔㔽惂䌮惛嚡惊溱Z抵⃑៷㸩Ⴣ䃃罋䃔橏⃏䃟惕栨惈䃄⃖媬⃂䃒⃚䃕Ⴧ状惎剎Ⴡ⃍ბR㲱㭄ᓷ㸾僝ი橛惗⃗䃋橒⩗დ穃Ὸ惄Ô惈牌გ惙ᙒ჎漭㰫瘲K僔С惙僔孏ᒰ栳獝灬ὅۧ᭏ᠱツ甤恄が僕チデ䀣ド彎キハパṎ㻨ũ槺灂罂㪠ᾨʤᢾ婀ᔺ⸨Ħ槴ᵼ烄犦䁈硉槮⿧㑄Ჵ槹䂼ੴ㖻媼罋ピビ縠࣑浀ࣔ炩≇⍍≂烈࣒网⍋Ĵ扖䉁࣋ᨠ䉊医䢻才ጲᔦࣉ੹卂匢⢨݂ବ⍀⬾䈾ジ⁺⽉ㆤ䣚ᾠ睕烒烚愦⤪4䣙ᶪ≋ܾ䣑䣅狮㦾䈡ਬ䣄忳䣊䣋䵂縭烎䣗䣛䣆ᠮ烂䣄ᏻ䣜䨢⠷ゲ䠳慘༺⣝ギ⣘ぇࣚ䃁⣄堩⣍籍⣖⣀੕ጼᚸ༬簯⣙⣋牷ࣔ䉔࣍籀棜࣐羯␶⠽໬帯嚺棖棈体ヅ⣘ࣘ⁁棄໪撶ᠦ棃棃⬫;棍渤㢽棏渻ࣘ棚䃋棝ᔳ棈ᣅ歜℺棇⎥䃓瞫棎ᣐࣅ棎࣑娱ᣝᐺ摍屖ᣃᣑ℺棐棐ᣏ棐棙棔ᣕ棞戫棈壌⁏ᣒ棏ᱚ棄ኧh屏棎壖Ꮶ翶䣝¶壂ኾ壍籋棉壘ᗫ⸧᭔ᠴ䵉ࢡ⣀㣟὘壂䩹単㣈彛⪲㣙⽍箹ᢩ略厽管㣌㣜橵⊯⽀瘧箹㣓烕呉㣇畤㧻Ꭶ燦絻Ꭵ㣕䱭㣅Ὀ硛㵸磁䞾坅䗡┣籕涳搯瑘ự磏箦灝㣃ਲ䦶橼啻㑎㡅琭瑑ၠ磩堿岼⠢ȶ᮰ɜ⠸Ӕӈ棜㣖媽磒悼Ӓӈ綡皤ɈӁ洴ӝᚰ咲砩溳ଵ粰䍑䒨栳Ӄ;ӏʷәᣄ壒ᐮӆ梪坞㸸䓅破䓔彎ᒬ⣃嚺䓋ӏ଴䓃Ӏ夭庥䓍癍磜磈䥛䓀ร㒣翬暽卐䓊暰䓋㬠ⵊ強ᚢⓕ➪䠺Ⓞ磔٬磇潔壊䓖Ⓤⓚ渽翲䪵ᚻ䓒ⓞⓌ声梷Ⓨⓒ⍣㱈擒ᇦ⍱ⓙ๹ⓗ䍕ⓜ㍌擜➢擋ⓓ翠䊾擌䍣䓞㸼侲怸∯ʠ磔擂ⓟ಻擖ᐵ磂罛潆擕ᣙ∠䓀夳擐ᓘ磉擄ⓞㅗⓀᓗᝈᓜⓊᓍ䈫睙幁梷ⓝᓌ䓆Ӗ⚲䓎擂Ⓡᓆሤ䈸Ⓣ䓋㚻ᓟ嵕ᓃ擎Ⓥ䓝ⓘᓖࣔᓓ㩉嚾擐ⓔ哛Ⓜʵ哝據៤䈯⡝䵑挲ᓃ擐ᒡ獍样䓅ⓜᓟ尢ⓘ㓍哌哇Ⓤ㓗哚哀卨獆Ⓤᓙ㓒擈z擙哟䓂Ⓧ㓎ᓜ哚樰㓉㓞㠻煗Ⓠ烠⌫粴瓁丯䗳ၑ哋媼㓅哂Ⓦ瓚䡯㓎㓊ᓉ瓀࣠ᵡ旤䓇㶿⣖咪㴭䓇瓚ӕ㣖ӏ䓈቏瓙㴠ೖܥ瓂嬳瓒೉ᡨ烉プἷパ೚䁓§ᑏ呆‸烖晗๋㍋䈻੎兎䰤摜䐡⿫੅ൗᖤ濩䶨ⶪً穀簱䄴䳌慆ຶ䳃䄲䳆㚻ᩒ摁೟ダ䣐抹೑㔿ృ⩛憷+⩏檭ᴳⱋರ牎晒皣ᐳ氧ᐻ✲縯僘䃏䝏䱀ⱍ቙ᴰⳟ䳈ŭⳖⳙ㽉破ⳉ簵⊢ⳓ㠥堣氦坕䐺橗ᙞⳐ僖擜䀹ⳅⳔሥ䱝ⳁ᛾泋Ⳅ犤ⳃ䱌ⳟⳇ婊⚪Ⳅ泘倶Ⳉ⃟僞፜䀮䱑⺩泖瘾況泑៼᳙泘Ⳁ礷Ⳅヒᐠ泋泘泒瑌泗僀僑Ⳇ亿䱂⼪᳙ᒫᨢ᳘罟娧䒨ⳁ夵泒ⱞ᳎吳泒怨泌㴥᳏泈Ⴠ᳐卙∧⒫䳀ረ峆橝獜娵᳝ᒯ᳘峈嚶᳍泏Ⳗ媱᳊峛泅᳏簿況Ⳟፉ峎䃅峓ሳ峖泃䣞䠭峇䣉㳓峚᳄峟峌峖桘㳚峚Ⳕ泎峂泃᳘椿⠹峓Ὂ椵㳏᳝峔ሼ⒦+峛憦糕᳞暧Ⳁ㳜峃㑟⩐泔㳋氱糂㳒泂㓆糊撡糁㳆䜢ニᚲ儶糜ቛ憾僔ˍ䥷峓᪳㳊಼Ⳓ峗㳇泜㳞峒㳑峝栤˙縶ܻ⪪˛˜˜㭀䜿ˎ糇ɋˌˑ糛Ⳙ䀮᳛㳉˓糇ᐵː糊㳓ˈ䋌ˑ䊬䋆ˈ˙䋊?᳆䥘䜢ブ˛栴峁˃泚ⶲⳙ᳋糀糝᳉䋙僎㭚怳䋞僄䋊㭎⋀⋍栨⋝泈㳖䋜⋞䋒⋘Ⴣˆ⋞㉟䋓䋈ⵧ䋟哂᬴撥⋁ᠾ˝⋖⚧㳎䋟㳜泊⋃ˀ㝍籘拊糞椼拄拏ⵌ拖撢䋅泊拐㳆拓⋆峋糁䋑拙卙招⪸拓䋛ᷤ″拐╄墵ᷠ䋍㿹糋㳑˔⋃糋⋞拍᳗⋙卆ዟ⊶㳏ዚዄ巶糎ዛ睄戰勂拓桅ዘ⋃⋝ዉ᳘ዛ⋁拇ዚ䃏ዔ㭘勌泒Ⓓ㳛㛪⒲糏㚺勚拁᳈ዏ㳗泉勁峙单⒤⒡皢㋛3䋚㋄勂ˈŮ㋗拆᳟勀ዐ㋎勄㳓ዘ倴ዙ勖擋ᔮ⒦㳌糍ᔠ狇峍拖ণ+勘Ợ狍㳏勊䋅糆䋃㋙˖峔㋝˜዆㠴糌潌滺狗勝⎻狆㋔勓ᓅᬯ狞㋖狚䋍ዝ糞勘㋛糍˗糃㽘૚⡝狞㳌狞వ䁀૚喱䁜⠲勍⋍㋂峑狎拄㋛ዌ㋚䃃૊撣૓䋌䫍ૄᓢ䫝㳏峕㋕糖拋㋚૑䋃˄䫁皺䫜絞େ୒䫚侦歋૟拞䫈㋅ˇ⋈䫏㋋䀫ཅἩ歜⫒怳䋗䫛䫆凪⫙㋃㳎䫁狂૓㋁勔泇㋄⫂㓀ᭁ皶⫙૜⁎⫁ᣑĪ〯䫙⫝̸૒婃ዝ⫀䫎Ⳍዌᣘ櫔⁖㳀櫟⫞櫄ૉ絥櫑⫖䫎狕ዄ⋕⫉狄ዘ⫕狎櫋䁁櫈狙徽櫓䋕㝐櫄䁲᫆䫎  "}



</details>
</li>
</ol>

The complete round-trip took 93.1 ms (including time required to validate the messages, start, and stop the internal mock server).

</details>

	

<hr>

<details>
<summary style="color:gray">Message schema (<code>request-file-analysis</code>)</summary>

For the definition of the hello message, please see it's implementation at [`./src/cli/repl/server/messages/message-analysis.ts`](https://github.com/flowr-analysis/flowr/tree/main/./src/cli/repl/server/messages/message-analysis.ts).

- (object)
    - **type** [required] _The type of the message._ (string)
        Only allows: 'request-file-analysis'
    - **id** [optional] _You may pass an id to link requests with responses (they get the same id)._ (string)
    - **filetoken** [optional] _A unique token to identify the file for subsequent requests. Only use this if you plan to send more queries!_ (string)
    - **filename** [optional] _A human-readable name of the file, only for debugging purposes._ (string)
    - **content** [optional] _The content of the file or an R expression (either give this or the filepath)._ (string)
    - **filepath** [optional] _The path to the file(s) on the local machine (either give this or the content)._ (alternatives)
        - (string)
        - (array)
        Valid item types:
            - (string)
    - **cfg** [optional] _If you want to extract the control flow information of the file._ (boolean)
    - **format** [optional] _The format of the results, if missing we assume json._ (string)
        Only allows: 'json', 'n-quads', 'compact'
    - **invalidateToken** [optional] _One or more file tokens to drop from the server store after this request has been answered._ (alternatives)
        - (string)
        - (array)
        Valid item types:
            - (string)

</details>

<details>
<summary style="color:gray">Message schema (<code>response-file-analysis</code>)</summary>

For the definition of the hello message, please see it's implementation at [`./src/cli/repl/server/messages/message-analysis.ts`](https://github.com/flowr-analysis/flowr/tree/main/./src/cli/repl/server/messages/message-analysis.ts).

- [required] _The response to a file analysis request (based on the `format` field)._ (alternatives)
    - _The response in JSON format._ (object)
        - **type** [required] _The type of the message._ (string)
            Only allows: 'response-file-analysis'
        - **id** [optional] _The id of the message, if you passed one in the request._ (string)
        - **format** [required] _The format of the results in json format._ (string)
            Only allows: 'json'
        - **results** [required] _The results of the analysis (one field per step)._ (object)
        - **cfg** [optional] _The control flow information of the file, only present if requested._ (object)
    - _The response as n-quads._ (object)
        - **type** [required] _The type of the message._ (string)
            Only allows: 'response-file-analysis'
        - **id** [optional] _The id of the message, if you passed one in the request._ (string)
        - **format** [required] _The format of the results in n-quads format._ (string)
            Only allows: 'n-quads'
        - **results** [required] _The results of the analysis (one field per step). Quads are presented as string._ (object)
        - **cfg** [optional] _The control flow information of the file, only present if requested._ (string)
    - (object)
        - **type** [required] _The type of the message._ (string)
            Only allows: 'response-file-analysis'
        - **id** [optional] _The id of the message, if you passed one in the request._ (string)
        - **format** [required] _The format of the results in bson format._ (string)
            Only allows: 'bson'
        - **results** [required] _The results of the analysis (one field per step)._ (string)
        - **cfg** [optional] _The control flow information of the file, only present if requested._ (string)

</details>



<hr>

</details>
	</li>

<li>
<a id="message-request-slice"></a>
<b>Slice</b> Message (<code>request-slice</code>) 
<details>

<summary style="color:gray"> View Details. <i>(<a href="https://github.com/flowr-analysis/flowr/wiki/Query%20API">deprecated</a>) The server slices a file based on the given criteria.</i> </summary>

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    autonumber
    participant Client
    participant Server

    
    Client->>+Server: request-slice

    alt
        Server-->>Client: response-slice
    else
        Server-->>Client: error
    end
    deactivate  Server
	
```


**We deprecated the slice request in favor of the `static-slice` [Query](https://github.com/flowr-analysis/flowr/wiki/query-api).**

To slice, you have to send a file analysis request first. The `filetoken` you assign is of use here as you can re-use it to repeatedly slice the same file.
Besides that, you only need to add an array of slicing criteria, using one of the formats described on the [terminology wiki page](https://github.com/flowr-analysis/flowr/wiki/Terminology#slicing-criterion) 
(however, instead of using `;`, you can simply pass separate array elements).
See the implementation of the request-slice message for more information.

Additionally, you may pass `"noMagicComments": true` to disable the automatic selection of elements based on magic comments (see below).


<details>
<summary>Example of the <code>request-slice</code> Message</summary>

_Note:_ even though we pretty-print these messages, they are sent as a single line, ending with a newline.

The following lists all messages that were sent and received in case you want to reproduce the scenario:

<ol>
<li> <code>hello</code> (response)
<details> 

<summary> Show Details </summary>

The first message is always a hello message.




```json
{
  "type": "hello",
  "clientName": "client-0",
  "versions": {
    "flowr": "2.12.3",
    "r": "4.6.1",
    "engine": "r-shell"
  }
}
```



</details>
</li>

<li> <code>request-file-analysis</code> (request)
<details> 

<summary> Show Details </summary>

Let's assume you want to slice the following script:

```r
x <- 1
x + 1
```


For this we first request the analysis, using a `filetoken` of `x` to slice the file in the next request.




```json
{
  "type": "request-file-analysis",
  "id": "1",
  "filetoken": "x",
  "content": "x <- 1\nx + 1"
}
```



</details>
</li>

<li> <code>response-file-analysis</code> (response)
<details> 

<summary> Show Details </summary>


See [above](#message-request-file-analysis) for the general structure of the response.
			


_As the code is pretty long, we inhibit pretty printing and syntax highlighting (JSON, hiding built-in):_

```text
{"type":"response-file-analysis","format":"json","id":"1","results":{"parse":{"files":[{"parsed":"[1,1,1,6,7,0,\"expr\",false,\"x <- 1\"],[1,1,1,1,1,3,\"SYMBOL\",true,\"x\"],[1,1,1,1,3,7,\"expr\",false,\"x\"],[1,3,1,4,2,7,\"LEFT_ASSIGN\",true,\"<-\"],[1,6,1,6,4,5,\"NUM_CONST\",true,\"1\"],[1,6,1,6,5,7,\"expr\",false,\"1\"],[2,1,2,5,16,0,\"expr\",false,\"x + 1\"],[2,1,2,1,10,12,\"SYMBOL\",true,\"x\"],[2,1,2,1,12,16,\"expr\",false,\"x\"],[2,3,2,3,11,16,\"'+'\",true,\"+\"],[2,5,2,5,13,14,\"NUM_CONST\",true,\"1\"],[2,5,2,5,14,16,\"expr\",false,\"1\"]","filePath":"/tmp/tmp-4041568-3snYBVfJfsnL-.R"}],".meta":{"timing":12}},"normalize":{"ast":{"type":"RProject","files":[{"root":{"type":"RExpressionList","children":[{"type":"RBinaryOp","location":[1,3,1,4],"lhs":{"type":"RSymbol","location":[1,1,1,1],"content":"x","lexeme":"x","info":{"fullRange":[1,1,1,1],"adToks":[],"id":0,"parent":2,"role":"bin-l","index":0,"nest":0,"file":"/tmp/tmp-4041568-3snYBVfJfsnL-.R"}},"rhs":{"location":[1,6,1,6],"lexeme":"1","info":{"fullRange":[1,6,1,6],"adToks":[],"id":1,"parent":2,"role":"bin-r","index":1,"nest":0,"file":"/tmp/tmp-4041568-3snYBVfJfsnL-.R"},"type":"RNumber","content":{"num":1,"complexNumber":false,"markedAsInt":false}},"operator":"<-","lexeme":"<-","info":{"fullRange":[1,1,1,6],"adToks":[],"id":2,"parent":6,"nest":0,"file":"/tmp/tmp-4041568-3snYBVfJfsnL-.R","index":0,"role":"el-c"}},{"type":"RBinaryOp","location":[2,3,2,3],"lhs":{"type":"RSymbol","location":[2,1,2,1],"content":"x","lexeme":"x","info":{"fullRange":[2,1,2,1],"adToks":[],"id":3,"parent":5,"role":"bin-l","index":0,"nest":0,"file":"/tmp/tmp-4041568-3snYBVfJfsnL-.R"}},"rhs":{"location":[2,5,2,5],"lexeme":"1","info":{"fullRange":[2,5,2,5],"adToks":[],"id":4,"parent":5,"role":"bin-r","index":1,"nest":0,"file":"/tmp/tmp-4041568-3snYBVfJfsnL-.R"},"type":"RNumber","content":{"num":1,"complexNumber":false,"markedAsInt":false}},"operator":"+","lexeme":"+","info":{"fullRange":[2,1,2,5],"adToks":[],"id":5,"parent":6,"nest":0,"file":"/tmp/tmp-4041568-3snYBVfJfsnL-.R","index":1,"role":"el-c"}}],"info":{"adToks":[],"id":6,"nest":0,"file":"/tmp/tmp-4041568-3snYBVfJfsnL-.R","role":"root","index":0}},"filePath":"/tmp/tmp-4041568-3snYBVfJfsnL-.R"}],"info":{"id":7}},".meta":{"timing":0}},"dataflow":{"unknownReferences":[],"in":[{"nodeId":2,"name":"<-","type":2},{"nodeId":5,"name":"+","t ```
```



</details>
</li>

<li> <b><code>request-slice</code> (request)</b>
<details open> 

<summary> Show Details </summary>

Of course, the second slice criterion `2:1` is redundant for the input, as they refer to the same variable. It is only for demonstration purposes.




```json
{
  "type": "request-slice",
  "id": "2",
  "filetoken": "x",
  "criterion": [
    "2@x",
    "2:1"
  ]
}
```



</details>
</li>

<li> <code>response-slice</code> (response)
<details> 

<summary> Show Details </summary>


The `results` field of the response contains two keys of importance:

- `slice`: which contains the result of the slicing (e.g., the ids included in the slice in `result`).
- `reconstruct`: contains the reconstructed code, as well as additional meta information. 
                   The automatically selected lines correspond to additional filters (e.g., magic comments) which force the unconditiojnal inclusion of certain elements.





```json
{
  "type": "response-slice",
  "id": "2",
  "results": {}
}
```



</details>
</li>
</ol>

The complete round-trip took 22.1 ms (including time required to validate the messages, start, and stop the internal mock server).

</details>


The semantics of the error message are similar. If, for example, the slicing criterion is invalid or the `filetoken` is unknown, _flowR_ will respond with an error.

&nbsp;

<a id="slice-magic-comments"></a>
**Magic Comments**


Within a document that is to be sliced, you can use magic comments to influence the slicing process:

- `# flowr@include_next_line` will cause the next line to be included, independent of if it is important for the slice.
- `# flowr@include_this_line` will cause the current line to be included, independent of if it is important for the slice.
- `# flowr@include_start` and `# flowr@include_end` will cause the lines between them to be included, independent of if they are important for the slice. These magic comments can be nested but should appear on a separate line.

	

<hr>

<details>
<summary style="color:gray">Message schema (<code>request-slice</code>)</summary>

For the definition of the hello message, please see it's implementation at [`./src/cli/repl/server/messages/message-slice.ts`](https://github.com/flowr-analysis/flowr/tree/main/./src/cli/repl/server/messages/message-slice.ts).

- (object)
    - **type** [required] _The type of the message._ (string)
        Only allows: 'request-slice'
    - **id** [optional] _The id of the message, if you passed one in the request._ (string)
    - **filetoken** [required] _The filetoken of the file to slice must be the same as with the analysis request._ (string)
    - **criterion** [required] _The slicing criteria to use._ (array)
    Valid item types:
        - (string)
    - **direction** _The direction to slice in. Defaults to backward slicing if unset._ (string)
        Only allows: 'backward', 'forward'

</details>

<details>
<summary style="color:gray">Message schema (<code>response-slice</code>)</summary>

For the definition of the hello message, please see it's implementation at [`./src/cli/repl/server/messages/message-slice.ts`](https://github.com/flowr-analysis/flowr/tree/main/./src/cli/repl/server/messages/message-slice.ts).

- _The response to a slice request._ (object)
    - **type** [required] _The type of the message._ (string)
        Only allows: 'response-slice'
    - **id** [optional] _The id of the message, if you passed one in the request._ (string)
    - **results** [required] _The results of the slice (one field per step slicing step)._ (object)

</details>



<hr>

</details>
	</li>

<li>
<a id="message-request-repl-execution"></a>
<b>REPL</b> Message (<code>request-repl-execution</code>) 
<details>

<summary style="color:gray"> View Details. <i>Access the read evaluate print loop of flowR.</i> </summary>

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    autonumber
    participant Client
    participant Server

    
    Client->>+Server: request-repl-execution

    alt
        Server-->>Client: error
    else

    loop
        Server-->>Client: response-repl-execution
    end
        Server-->>Client: end-repl-execution

    end

    deactivate  Server
	
```


> [!WARNING]
> To execute arbitrary R commands with a request, the server has to be started explicitly with <span title="Description (Command Line Argument): Allow to access the underlying R session when using flowR (security warning: this allows the execution of arbitrary R code!)">`--r-session-access`</span>.
> Please be aware that this introduces a security risk.


The REPL execution message allows to send a REPL command to receive its output. 
For more on the REPL, see the [introduction](https://github.com/flowr-analysis/flowr/wiki/overview#the-read-eval-print-loop-repl), or the [description below](#using-the-repl).
You only have to pass the command you want to execute in the `expression` field. 
Furthermore, you can set the `ansi` field to `true` if you are interested in output formatted using [ANSI escape codes](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ANSI_escape_code).
We strongly recommend you to make use of the `id` field to link answers with requests as you can theoretically request the execution of multiple scripts at the same time, which then happens in parallel.

> [!WARNING]
> There is currently no automatic sandboxing or safeguarding against such requests. They simply execute the respective&nbsp;R code on your machine. 
> Please be very careful (and do not use <span title="Description (Command Line Argument): Allow to access the underlying R session when using flowR (security warning: this allows the execution of arbitrary R code!)">`--r-session-access`</span> if you are unsure).


The answer on such a request is different from the other messages as the `response-repl-execution` message may be sent multiple times. 
This allows to better handle requests that require more time but already output intermediate results.
You can detect the end of the execution by receiving the `end-repl-execution` message.

The semantics of the error message are similar to that of the other messages.

<details>
<summary>Example of the <code>request-slice</code> Message</summary>

_Note:_ even though we pretty-print these messages, they are sent as a single line, ending with a newline.

The following lists all messages that were sent and received in case you want to reproduce the scenario:

<ol>
<li> <code>hello</code> (response)
<details> 

<summary> Show Details </summary>

The first message is always a hello message.




```json
{
  "type": "hello",
  "clientName": "client-0",
  "versions": {
    "flowr": "2.12.3",
    "r": "4.6.1",
    "engine": "r-shell"
  }
}
```



</details>
</li>

<li> <b><code>request-repl-execution</code> (request)</b>
<details open> 

<summary> Show Details </summary>






```json
{
  "type": "request-repl-execution",
  "id": "1",
  "expression": ":help"
}
```



</details>
</li>

<li> <code>response-repl-execution</code> (response)
<details> 

<summary> Show Details </summary>


The `stream` field (either `stdout` or `stderr`) informs you of the output's origin: either the standard output or the standard error channel. After this message follows the end marker.


<details>
<summary>Pretty-Printed Result</summary>


```text

If enabled ('--r-session-access' and if using the 'r-shell' engine), you can just enter R expressions which get evaluated right away:
R> 1 + 1
[1] 2

Besides that, you can use the following commands. The scripts can accept further arguments. In general, those ending with [*] may be called with and without the star. 
There are the following basic commands:
  :controlflow[*]     Get mermaid code for the control-flow graph of R code (star: Returns the URL to mermaid.live) (aliases: :cfg, :cf)
     variants: :controlflowbb[*] (:cfgb, :cfb)
  :dataflow[*]        Get mermaid code for the dataflow graph (star: Returns the URL to mermaid.live) (aliases: :d, :df)
     variants: :dataflowascii (:df!), :dataflowsilent (:d#, :df#), :dataflowsimple[*] (:ds, :dfs)
  :execute            Execute the given code as R code. This requires the `--r-session-access` flag to be set and requires the r-shell engine. (aliases: :e, :r)
  :help               Show help information (aliases: :h, :?)
  :normalize[*]       Get mermaid code for the normalized AST of R code (star: Returns the URL to mermaid.live) (alias: :n)
     variants: :normalize# (:n#)
  :parse              Prints ASCII Art of the parsed, unmodified AST (alias: :p)
  :query[*]           Query the given R code (use 'help' for more information) (star: Similar to query, but returns the output in json format.)
  :quit               End the repl (aliases: :q, :exit)
  :signature          Inspect and extend the signature database: `query` (identical to :query @signature), `add <path>` to mount another database/source, `download` to fetch the full-history database. (alias: :sig)
  :version            Prints the version of flowR as well as the current version of R

Furthermore, you can directly call the following scripts which accept arguments. If you are unsure, try to add --help after the command.
  :benchmark          Benchmark the static backwards slicer
  :export-quads       Export quads of the normalized AST of a given R code file
  :slicer             Static backwards executable slicer for R
  :summarizer         Summarize the results of the benchmark

You can combine commands by separating them with a semicolon ;.

Commands that accept a file path support two path prefixes:
  file://<path>   run the command once on the given file or folder
  watch://<path>  re-run the command whenever the file (or any file in the folder) changes
                     Press Ctrl+C or enter any other command to leave watch mode.

You are running flowR v2.12.3 (use :version for details). Check for newer releases and per-install upgrade steps (Docker, npm, source) at:
  https://github.com/flowr-analysis/flowr/releases
```


</details>

```json
  "id": "1",
  "result": "\nIf enabled ('--r-session-access' and if using the 'r-shell' engine), you can just enter R expressions which get evaluated right away:\nR> 1 + 1\n[1] 2\n\nBesides that, you can use the following commands.   "stream": "stdout"
```

<details>
<summary style="color:gray">Message schema (<code>request-repl-execution</code>)</summary>

For the definition of the hello message, please see it's implementation at [`./src/cli/repl/server/messages/message-repl.ts`](https://github.com/flowr-analysis/flowr/tree/main/./src/cli/repl/server/messages/message-repl.ts).

- (object)
    - **type** [required] _The type of the message._ (string)
        Only allows: 'request-repl-execution'
    - **id** [optional] _The id of the message, will be the same for the request._ (string)
    - **ansi** [optional] _Should ansi formatting be enabled for the response? Is `false` by default._ (boolean)
    - **expression** [required] _The expression to execute._ (string)

</details>

<details>
<summary style="color:gray">Message schema (<code>response-repl-execution</code>)</summary>

For the definition of the hello message, please see it's implementation at [`./src/cli/repl/server/messages/message-repl.ts`](https://github.com/flowr-analysis/flowr/tree/main/./src/cli/repl/server/messages/message-repl.ts).

- (object)
    - **type** [required] _The type of the message._ (string)
        Only allows: 'response-repl-execution'
    - **id** [optional] _The id of the message, will be the same for the request._ (string)
    - **stream** [required] _The stream the message is from._ (string)
        Only allows: 'stdout', 'stderr'
    - **result** [required] _The output of the execution._ (string)

</details>

- (object)
    - **type** [required] _The type of the message._ (string)
        Only allows: 'end-repl-execution'
    - **id** [optional] _The id of the message, will be the same for the request._ (string)

<li>
<a id="message-request-query"></a>
<b>Query</b> Message (<code>request-query</code>) 
<details>

<summary style="color:gray"> View Details. <i>Query an analysis result for specific information.</i> </summary>

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    autonumber
    participant Client
    participant Server

    
    Client->>+Server: request-query

    alt
        Server-->>Client: response-query
    else
        Server-->>Client: error
    end
    deactivate  Server
	
```


To send queries, you have to send an [analysis request](#message-request-file-analysis) first. The `filetoken` you assign is of use here as you can re-use it to repeatedly query the same file.
This message provides direct access to _flowR_'s Query API. Please consult the [Query API documentation](https://github.com/flowr-analysis/flowr/wiki/query-api) for more information.


<details>
<summary>Example of the <code>request-query</code> Message</summary>

_Note:_ even though we pretty-print these messages, they are sent as a single line, ending with a newline.

The following lists all messages that were sent and received in case you want to reproduce the scenario:

<ol>
<li> <code>hello</code> (response)
<details> 

<summary> Show Details </summary>

The first message is always a hello message.




```json
{
  "type": "hello",
  "clientName": "client-0",
  "versions": {
    "flowr": "2.12.3",
    "r": "4.6.1",
    "engine": "r-shell"
  }
}
```



</details>
</li>

<li> <code>request-file-analysis</code> (request)
<details> 

<summary> Show Details </summary>

Let's assume you want to query the following script:

```r
library(ggplot)
library(dplyr)
library(readr)

# read data with read_csv
data <- read_csv('data.csv')
data2 <- read_csv('data2.csv')

m <- mean(data$x) 
print(m)

data %>%
	ggplot(aes(x = x, y = y)) +
	geom_point()
	
plot(data2$x, data2$y)
points(data2$x, data2$y)
	
print(mean(data2$k))
```
.

For this we first request the analysis, using a dummy `filetoken` of `x` to slice the file in the next request.




```json
{
  "type": "request-file-analysis",
  "id": "1",
  "filetoken": "x",
  "content": "library(ggplot)\nlibrary(dplyr)\nlibrary(readr)\n\n# read data with read_csv\ndata <- read_csv('data.csv')\ndata2 <- read_csv('data2.csv')\n\nm <- mean(data$x) \nprint(m)\n\ndata %>%\n\tggplot(aes(x = x, y = y)) +\n\tgeom_point()\n\t\nplot(data2$x, data2$y)\npoints(data2$x, data2$y)\n\t\nprint(mean(data2$k))"
}
```



</details>
</li>

<li> <code>response-file-analysis</code> (response)
<details> 

<summary> Show Details </summary>


See [above](#message-request-file-analysis) for the general structure of the response.
			


_As the code is pretty long, we inhibit pretty printing and syntax highlighting (JSON, hiding built-in):_

<details>
<summary style="color:gray">Message schema (<code>request-query</code>)</summary>

For the definition of the hello message, please see it's implementation at [`./src/cli/repl/server/messages/message-query.ts`](https://github.com/flowr-analysis/flowr/tree/main/./src/cli/repl/server/messages/message-query.ts).

- _Request a query to be run on the file analysis information._ (object)
    - **type** [required] _The type of the message._ (string)
        Only allows: 'request-query'
    - **id** [optional] _If you give the id, the response will be sent to the client with the same id._ (string)
    - **filetoken** [required] _The filetoken of the file/data retrieved from the analysis request._ (string)
    - **query** [required] _The query to run on the file analysis information._ (array)
    Valid item types:
        - _A virtual or an active query!_ (alternatives)
            - _Supported queries_ (alternatives)
                - _Call context query used to find calls in the dataflow graph_ (object)
                    - **type** [required] _The type of the query._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'call-context'
                    - **callName** [required] _Regex regarding the function name!_ (string)
                    - **callNameExact** [optional] _Should we automatically add the `^` and `$` anchors to the regex to make it an exact match?_ (boolean)
                    - **kind** [optional] _The kind of the call, this can be used to group calls together (e.g., linking `plot` to `visualize`). Defaults to `.`_ (string)
                    - **subkind** [optional] _The subkind of the call, this can be used to uniquely identify the respective call type when grouping the output (e.g., the normalized name, linking `ggplot` to `plot`). Defaults to `.`_ (string)
                    - **callTargets** [optional] _Call targets the function may have. This defaults to `any`. Request this specifically to gain all call targets we can resolve._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'global', 'must-include-global', 'local', 'must-include-local', 'any'
                    - **callTargetNamespace** [optional] _Only keep calls that resolve to (or are explicitly qualified with) this package (e.g. `bar` to find `bar::foo`)._ (string)
                    - **ignoreParameterValues** [optional] _Should we ignore default values for parameters in the results?_ (boolean)
                    - **includeAliases** [optional] _Consider a case like `f <- function_of_interest`, do you want uses of `f` to be included in the results?_ (boolean)
                    - **fileFilter** [optional] _Filter that, when set, a node's file attribute must match to be considered_ (object)
                        - **fileFilter** [required] _Regex that a node's file attribute must match to be considered_ (string)
                        - **includeUndefinedFiles** [optional] _If `fileFilter` is set, but a nodes `file` attribute is `undefined`, should we include it in the results? Defaults to `true`._ (boolean)
                    - **linkTo** [optional] _Links the current call to the last call of the given kind. This way, you can link a call like `points` to the latest graphics plot etc._ (alternatives)
                        - (alternatives)
                            - _Links the current call to the last call of the given kind. This way, you can link a call like `points` to the latest graphics plot etc._ (object)
                                - **type** [required] _The type of the linkTo sub-query._ (string)
                                    Only allows: 'link-to-last-call'
                                - **callName** [required] _Test regarding the function name of the last call. Similar to `callName`, strings are interpreted as a regular expression, and string arrays are checked for containment._ (alternatives)
                                    - (string)
                                    - (array)
                                    Valid item types:
                                        - (string)
                                - **ignoreIf** [optional] _Should we ignore this (source) call? Currently, there is no well working serialization for this._ (function)
                                - **cascadeIf** [optional] _Should we continue searching after the link was created? Currently, there is no well working serialization for this._ (function)
                                - **attachLinkInfo** [optional] _Additional information to attach to the link._ (object)
                            - _Allows to link nested calls to their parent calls. This way, you can link an `assert_equal` call to the parent `test_that` call etc._ (object)
                                - **type** [required] _The type of the linkTo sub-query._ (string)
                                    Only allows: 'link-to-nested-call'
                                - **callName** [required] _Test regarding the function name of the last call. Similar to `callName`, strings are interpreted as a regular expression, and string arrays are checked for containment._ (alternatives)
                                    - (string)
                                    - (array)
                                    Valid item types:
                                        - (string)
                                - **ignoreIf** [optional] _Should we ignore this (source) call? Currently, there is no well working serialization for this._ (function)
                                - **attachLinkInfo** [optional] _Additional information to attach to the link._ (object)
                        - (array)
                        Valid item types:
                            - (alternatives)
                                - _Links the current call to the last call of the given kind. This way, you can link a call like `points` to the latest graphics plot etc._ (object)
                                    - **type** [required] _The type of the linkTo sub-query._ (string)
                                        Only allows: 'link-to-last-call'
                                    - **callName** [required] _Test regarding the function name of the last call. Similar to `callName`, strings are interpreted as a regular expression, and string arrays are checked for containment._ (alternatives)
                                        - (string)
                                        - (array)
                                        Valid item types:
                                            - (string)
                                    - **ignoreIf** [optional] _Should we ignore this (source) call? Currently, there is no well working serialization for this._ (function)
                                    - **cascadeIf** [optional] _Should we continue searching after the link was created? Currently, there is no well working serialization for this._ (function)
                                    - **attachLinkInfo** [optional] _Additional information to attach to the link._ (object)
                                - _Allows to link nested calls to their parent calls. This way, you can link an `assert_equal` call to the parent `test_that` call etc._ (object)
                                    - **type** [required] _The type of the linkTo sub-query._ (string)
                                        Only allows: 'link-to-nested-call'
                                    - **callName** [required] _Test regarding the function name of the last call. Similar to `callName`, strings are interpreted as a regular expression, and string arrays are checked for containment._ (alternatives)
                                        - (string)
                                        - (array)
                                        Valid item types:
                                            - (string)
                                    - **ignoreIf** [optional] _Should we ignore this (source) call? Currently, there is no well working serialization for this._ (function)
                                    - **attachLinkInfo** [optional] _Additional information to attach to the link._ (object)
                - _The config query retrieves the current configuration of the flowR instance and optionally also updates it._ (object)
                    - **type** [required] _The type of the query._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'config'
                    - **update** [optional] _An optional partial configuration to update the current configuration with before returning it. Only the provided fields will be updated, all other fields will remain unchanged._ (object)
                    - **inspect** [optional] _An optional `.`-separated path (as a string array) to read a single configuration value instead of returning the whole configuration._ (array)
                    Valid item types:
                        - (string)
                - _The control flow query provides the control flow graph of the analysis, optionally simplified._ (object)
                    - **type** [required] _The type of the query._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'control-flow'
                    - **config** [optional] _Optional configuration for the control flow query._ (object)
                        - **simplificationPasses** _The simplification passes to apply to the control flow graph. If unset, the default simplification order will be used._ (array)
                        Valid item types:
                            - (string)
                                Only allows: 'unique-cf-sets', 'analyze-dead-code', 'remove-dead-code', 'to-basic-blocks'
                - _A query to compute the Call Graph of the analyzed project._ (object)
                    - **type** [required] _The type of the query._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'call-graph'
                    - **expandLibraryInternals** [optional] _Expand library/built-in leaf calls into their internal callees via the signature database (default false)._ (boolean)
                - _The dataflow query simply returns the dataflow graph, there is no need to pass it multiple times!_ (object)
                    - **type** [required] _The type of the query._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'dataflow'
                - _Either returns all function definitions alongside whether they are recursive, or just those matching the filters._ (object)
                    - **type** [required] _The type of the query._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'does-call'
                    - **queryId** [optional] _An optional unique identifier for this query, to identify it in the output._ (string)
                    - **call** _The function from which calls are being made. This is a slicing criterion that resolves to a function definition node._ (string)
                    - **calls** [required] _The constraints on which functions are being called. This can be a combination of name-based or id-based constraints, combined with logical operators (and, or, one-of)._ (object)
                    - **expandLibraryInternals** [optional] _Expand a reached library/built-in leaf call into its internal callees via the signature database and match constraints against those too (default false)._ (boolean)
                - _The dataflow-lens query returns a simplified view on the dataflow graph_ (object)
                    - **type** [required] _The type of the query._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'dataflow-lens'
                - _The abstract interpretation query retrieves inferred abstract values_ (object)
                    - **type** [required] _The type of the query._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'absint'
                    - **inference** [required] _The type of abstract interpretation inference._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'df-shape'
                    - **criteria** [optional] _The slicing criteria of the nodes to get the inferred abstract values for._ (array)
                    Valid item types:
                        - (string)
                - _The file query finds files in the project based on their roles and path patterns._ (object)
                    - **type** [required] _The type of the query._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'files'
                    - **roles** [optional] _Optional roles of the files to query. If not provided, all roles are considered._ (array)
                    Valid item types:
                        - (string)
                            Only allows: 'description', 'namespace', 'news', 'vignette', 'test', 'install', 'data', 'license', 'virtual-env', 'manifest', 'source', 'other'
                    - **matchesPathRegex** [optional] _An optional regular expression to match the file paths against._ (string)
                - _The id map query retrieves the id map from the normalized AST._ (object)
                    - **type** [required] _The type of the query._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'id-map'
                - _The normalized AST query simply returns the normalized AST, there is no need to pass it multiple times!_ (object)
                    - **type** [required] _The type of the query._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'normalized-ast'
                - _The cluster query calculates and returns all clusters in the dataflow graph._ (object)
                    - **type** [required] _The type of the query._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'dataflow-cluster'
                - _Slice query used to slice the dataflow graph_ (object)
                    - **type** [required] _The type of the query._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'static-slice'
                    - **criteria** [required] _The slicing criteria to use._ (array)
                    Valid item types:
                        - (string)
                    - **direction** [optional] _The direction to slice in. Defaults to backward slicing if unset._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'backward', 'forward'
                    - **noReconstruction** [optional] _Do not reconstruct the slice into readable code._ (boolean)
                    - **noMagicComments** [optional] _Should the magic comments (force-including lines within the slice) be ignored?_ (boolean)
                    - **inlineSources** [optional] _Inline resolvable source() calls into the reconstruction so the result is a single self-contained R text._ (boolean)
                    - **inlineFull** [optional] _Inline all files into the reconstruction, in flowR's loading order and independent of whether they are sourced explicitly; "banner" precedes every file with a banner comment naming it._ (alternatives)
                        - (boolean)
                        - (string)
                            Only allows: 'banner'
                    - **includeCallees** [optional] _If set (and slicing backward), continue the slice past a function-definition boundary, also including the definition's binding and call sites._ (boolean)
                - _Provenance query definition_ (object)
                    - **type** [required] _The type of the query._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'provenance'
                    - **criterion** [required] _The slicing criterion to use._ (string)
                    - **restrictFdef** [required] _Whether to stop on fdef boundaries._ (boolean)
                - _Input Sources query definition_ (object)
                    - **type** [required] _The type of the query._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'input-sources'
                    - **criterion** [required] _The slicing criterion or array of criteria to use._ (alternatives)
                        - (string)
                        - (array)
                        Valid item types:
                            - (string)
                    - **config** [optional] (object)
                        - **pure** [optional] _Deterministic/pure functions: functions that preserve constantness of their inputs (e.g., arithmetic, parse)._ (array)
                        Valid item types:
                            - (string)
                        - **file** [optional] _Functions that read from the filesystem and produce data (e.g., read.csv, readRDS)._ (array)
                        Valid item types:
                            - (string)
                        - **tempfile** [optional] _Functions that produce temporary file paths (sub-type of File; e.g., tempfile, tempdir)._ (array)
                        Valid item types:
                            - (string)
                        - **net** [optional] _Functions that fetch data from the network (e.g., download.file, url connections)._ (array)
                        Valid item types:
                            - (string)
                        - **rand** [optional] _Functions that produce randomness (e.g., runif, rnorm)._ (array)
                        Valid item types:
                            - (string)
                        - **system** [optional] _Functions that execute system commands (e.g., system, system2, shell, pipe)._ (array)
                        Valid item types:
                            - (string)
                        - **ffi** [optional] _Functions that call native code via the R FFI (.C, .Call, .Fortran, .External, dyn.load)._ (array)
                        Valid item types:
                            - (string)
                        - **lang** [optional] _Functions that produce language objects (e.g., substitute, quote, bquote, expression)._ (array)
                        Valid item types:
                            - (string)
                        - **options** [optional] _Functions that access or set global options (e.g., options, getOption)._ (array)
                        Valid item types:
                            - (string)
                        - **user** [optional] _Functions that read interactive user input (e.g., file.choose, readline, menu, askYesNo)._ (array)
                        Valid item types:
                            - (string)
                - _The dependencies query retrieves and returns the set of all dependencies in the dataflow graph, which includes libraries, sourced files, read data, and written data._ (object)
                    - **type** [required] _The type of the query._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'dependencies'
                    - **ignoreDefaultFunctions** [optional] _Should the set of functions that are detected by default be ignored/skipped? Defaults to false._ (boolean)
                    - **libraryFunctions** [optional] _The set of library functions to search for._ (array)
                    Valid item types:
                        - (object)
                            - **name** [required] _The name of the library function._ (string)
                            - **package** [optional] _The package name of the library function_ (string)
                            - **argIdx** [optional] _The index of the argument that contains the library name._ (number)
                            - **argName** [optional] _The name of the argument that contains the library name._ (string)
                    - **sourceFunctions** [optional] _The set of source functions to search for._ (array)
                    Valid item types:
                        - (object)
                            - **name** [required] _The name of the library function._ (string)
                            - **package** [optional] _The package name of the library function_ (string)
                            - **argIdx** [optional] _The index of the argument that contains the library name._ (number)
                            - **argName** [optional] _The name of the argument that contains the library name._ (string)
                    - **readFunctions** [optional] _The set of read functions to search for._ (array)
                    Valid item types:
                        - (object)
                            - **name** [required] _The name of the library function._ (string)
                            - **package** [optional] _The package name of the library function_ (string)
                            - **argIdx** [optional] _The index of the argument that contains the library name._ (number)
                            - **argName** [optional] _The name of the argument that contains the library name._ (string)
                    - **writeFunctions** [optional] _The set of write functions to search for._ (array)
                    Valid item types:
                        - (object)
                            - **name** [required] _The name of the library function._ (string)
                            - **package** [optional] _The package name of the library function_ (string)
                            - **argIdx** [optional] _The index of the argument that contains the library name._ (number)
                            - **argName** [optional] _The name of the argument that contains the library name._ (string)
                    - **visualizeFunctions** [optional] _The set of visualize functions to search for._ (array)
                    Valid item types:
                        - (object)
                            - **name** [required] _The name of the library function._ (string)
                            - **package** [optional] _The package name of the library function_ (string)
                            - **argIdx** [optional] _The index of the argument that contains the library name._ (number)
                            - **argName** [optional] _The name of the argument that contains the library name._ (string)
                    - **testFunctions** [optional] _The set of test functions to search for._ (array)
                    Valid item types:
                        - (object)
                            - **name** [required] _The name of the library function._ (string)
                            - **package** [optional] _The package name of the library function_ (string)
                            - **argIdx** [optional] _The index of the argument that contains the library name._ (number)
                            - **argName** [optional] _The name of the argument that contains the library name._ (string)
                    - **undeclaredFunctions** [optional] _The set of undeclared functions to search for._ (array)
                    Valid item types:
                        - (object)
                            - **name** [required] _The name of the library function._ (string)
                            - **package** [optional] _The package name of the library function_ (string)
                            - **argIdx** [optional] _The index of the argument that contains the library name._ (number)
                            - **argName** [optional] _The name of the argument that contains the library name._ (string)
                    - **unusedFunctions** [optional] _The set of unused functions to search for._ (array)
                    Valid item types:
                        - (object)
                            - **name** [required] _The name of the library function._ (string)
                            - **package** [optional] _The package name of the library function_ (string)
                            - **argIdx** [optional] _The index of the argument that contains the library name._ (number)
                            - **argName** [optional] _The name of the argument that contains the library name._ (string)
                    - **enabledCategories** [optional] _A set of flags that determines what types of dependencies are searched for. If unset, all dependency types are searched for._ (array)
                    Valid item types:
                        - (string)
                    - **additionalCategories** [optional] _A set of additional, user-supplied dependency categories, whose results will be included in the query return value._ (object)
                        Only allows: '[object Object]'
                - _The location map query retrieves the location of every id in the ast._ (object)
                    - **type** [required] _The type of the query._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'location-map'
                    - **ids** [optional] _Optional list of ids to filter the results by._ (array)
                    Valid item types:
                        - (string)
                - _The search query searches the normalized AST and dataflow graph for nodes that match the given search query._ (object)
                    - **type** [required] _The type of the query._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'search'
                    - **search** [required] _The search query to execute._ (object)
                - _Happens-Before tracks whether a always happens before b._ (object)
                    - **type** [required] _The type of the query._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'happens-before'
                    - **a** [required] _The first slicing criterion._ (string)
                    - **b** [required] _The second slicing criterion._ (string)
                - _Query to inspect which functions throw exceptions._ (object)
                    - **type** [required] _The type of the query._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'inspect-exception'
                    - **filter** [optional] _If given, only function definitions that match one of the given slicing criteria are considered. Each criterion can be either `line:column`, `line@variable-name`, or `$id`, where the latter directly specifies the node id of the function definition to be considered._ (array)
                    Valid item types:
                        - [required] (string)
                - _Either returns all function definitions alongside whether they are higher-order functions, or just those matching the filters._ (object)
                    - **type** [required] _The type of the query._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'inspect-higher-order'
                    - **filter** [optional] _If given, only function definitions that match one of the given slicing criteria are considered. Each criterion can be either `line:column`, `line@variable-name`, or `$id`, where the latter directly specifies the node id of the function definition to be considered._ (array)
                    Valid item types:
                        - [required] (string)
                - _Either returns all function definitions alongside whether they are recursive, or just those matching the filters._ (object)
                    - **type** [required] _The type of the query._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'inspect-recursion'
                    - **filter** [optional] _If given, only function definitions that match one of the given slicing criteria are considered. Each criterion can be either `line:column`, `line@variable-name`, or `$id`, where the latter directly specifies the node id of the function definition to be considered._ (array)
                    Valid item types:
                        - [required] (string)
                - _The resolve value query used to get definitions of an identifier_ (object)
                    - **type** [required] _The type of the query._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'resolve-value'
                    - **criteria** [required] _The slicing criteria to use._ (array)
                    Valid item types:
                        - (string)
                - _The project query provides information on the analyzed project._ (object)
                    - **type** [required] _The type of the query._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'project'
                    - **withDf** [optional] _Whether to include Dataflow information in the result._ (boolean)
                - _Inspects the loaded signature database(s): loaded databases, a package, a function, or wildcard matches (optionally filtered by parameter name or required-parameter count)._ (object)
                    - **type** [required] _The type of the query._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'signature'
                    - **package** [optional] _The package to inspect (glob wildcards allowed); omit for a summary of the loaded databases._ (string)
                    - **function** [optional] _A function/symbol to inspect (glob wildcards allowed)._ (string)
                    - **version** [optional] _A version spec: an exact version, a glob (3.*), a semver range (>=3.0.0, 3.x), or a release-date bound (<=2026, >=2021.05 in YYYY.MM.DD)._ (string)
                    - **parameters** [optional] _Keep only functions that have a parameter matching every one of these names (glob wildcards allowed, position-independent)._ (array)
                    Valid item types:
                        - (string)
                    - **requiredParameters** [optional] _Keep only functions with exactly this many required (no-default) parameters, excluding `...`._ (number)
                    - **callGraph** [optional] _For a single function, also render its transitive call graph as a mermaid.live link (`--cg`)._ (boolean)
                - _The resolve value query used to get definitions of an identifier_ (object)
                    - **type** [required] _The type of the query._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'origin'
                    - **criterion** [required] _The slicing criteria to use_ (string)
                - _The linter query lints for the given set of rules and returns the result._ (object)
                    - **type** [required] _The type of the query._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'linter'
                    - **format** [optional] _Print the findings in a machine-readable format instead of the human-readable summary._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'text', 'sarif', 'github'
                    - **rules** _The rules to lint for. If unset, all rules will be included._ (array)
                    Valid item types:
                        - (string)
                            Only allows: 'deprecated-functions', 'file-path-validity', 'seeded-randomness', 'absolute-file-paths', 'unused-definitions', 'naming-convention', 'network-functions', 'dataframe-access-validation', 'dead-code', 'useless-loop', 'problematic-inputs', 'stop-call', 'roxygen-arguments', 'software-has-license', 'software-has-tests', 'no-leaked-credentials', 'undefined-symbol'
                        - (object)
                            - **name** [required] (string)
                                Only allows: 'deprecated-functions', 'file-path-validity', 'seeded-randomness', 'absolute-file-paths', 'unused-definitions', 'naming-convention', 'network-functions', 'dataframe-access-validation', 'dead-code', 'useless-loop', 'problematic-inputs', 'stop-call', 'roxygen-arguments', 'software-has-license', 'software-has-tests', 'no-leaked-credentials', 'undefined-symbol'
                            - **config** (object)
                - _Dice query: selects only paths from the given start nodes that reach the given end nodes._ (object)
                    - **type** [required] _The type of the query._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'dice'
                    - **from** [required] _Slicing criteria for the start of the dice (forward slice seeds)._ (array)
                    Valid item types:
                        - (string)
                    - **to** [required] _Slicing criteria for the end of the dice (backward slice seeds)._ (array)
                    Valid item types:
                        - (string)
                    - **noReconstruction** [optional] _Do not reconstruct the slice into readable code._ (boolean)
                    - **noMagicComments** [optional] _Should the magic comments (force-including lines within the slice) be ignored?_ (boolean)
                    - **inlineSources** [optional] _Inline resolvable source() calls into the reconstruction so the result is a single self-contained R text._ (boolean)
                    - **inlineFull** [optional] _Inline all files into the reconstruction, in flowR's loading order and independent of whether they are sourced explicitly; "banner" precedes every file with a banner comment naming it._ (alternatives)
                        - (boolean)
                        - (string)
                            Only allows: 'banner'
                    - **includeCallees** [optional] _If set (and slicing backward), continue the slice past a function-definition boundary, also including the definition's binding and call sites._ (boolean)
                - _Guesses the possible version range of every dependency from declared constraints and signature-database usage._ (object)
                    - **type** [required] _The type of the query._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'guess-dep-versions'
                    - **packages** [optional] _Restrict the guess to these packages; omit to guess for every declared and used dependency._ (array)
                    Valid item types:
                        - (string)
                    - **date** [optional] _Only consider versions released on or before this day, written YYYY.MM.DD (also YYYY or YYYY.MM)._ (string)
                    - **maxCandidates** [optional] _Cap the number of candidate versions listed per dependency._ (number)
                    - **clean** [optional] _Ignore the project declared constraints (DESCRIPTION/lockfile/transitive); guess purely from code usage and the date/R bounds._ (boolean)
                    - **explode** [optional] _Also explode the guessed space into concrete per-dependency version assignments._ (object)
                        - **order** [optional] _Iterate each dependency newest-first (default) or oldest-first._ (string)
                            Only allows: 'newest', 'oldest'
                        - **prefer** [optional] _A version to prefer per dependency when it survives the constraints._ (object)
                        - **limit** [optional] _Cap the number of concrete assignments produced._ (number)
            - _Virtual queries (used for structure)_ (alternatives)
                - _Compound query used to combine queries of the same type_ (object)
                    - **type** [required] _The type of the query._ (string)
                        Only allows: 'compound'
                    - **query** [required] _The query to run on the file analysis information._ (string)
                    - **commonArguments** [required] _Common arguments for all queries._ (object)
                    - **arguments** [required] _Arguments for each query._ (array)
                    Valid item types:
                        - (object)

</details>

<details>
<summary style="color:gray">Message schema (<code>response-query</code>)</summary>

For the definition of the hello message, please see it's implementation at [`./src/cli/repl/server/messages/message-query.ts`](https://github.com/flowr-analysis/flowr/tree/main/./src/cli/repl/server/messages/message-query.ts).

- _The response to a query request._ (object)
    - **type** [required] (string)
        Only allows: 'response-query'
    - **id** [optional] _The id of the message, will be the same for the request._ (string)
    - **results** [required] _The results of the query._ (object)

</details>

</details>
	</li>

</ul>

### 📡 Ways of Connecting

If you are interested in clients that communicate with _flowR_, please check out the [R adapter](https://github.com/flowr-analysis/flowr-r-adapter)
as well as the [Visual Studio Code extension](https://github.com/flowr-analysis/vscode-flowr).

<ol>

<li>
<a id="using-netcat-without-websocket"></a>Using Netcat

<details>

<summary>Without Websocket</summary>

Suppose, you want to launch the server using a docker container. Then, start the server by (forwarding the internal default port):


```shell
docker run -p1042:1042 -it --rm eagleoutice/flowr --server
```


Now, using a tool like [_netcat_](https://linux.die.net/man/1/nc) to connect:


```shell
nc 127.0.0.1 1042
```


Within the started session, type the following message (as a single line) and press enter to see the response:


```json
{"type":"request-file-analysis","content":"x <- 1","id":"1"}
```


</details>
</li>

<li> Using Python
<details>
<summary>Without Websocket</summary>

In Python, a similar process would look like this. After starting the server as with using [netcat](#using-netcat-without-websocket), you can use the following script to connect:


```python

import socket

with socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM) as s:
    s.connect(('127.0.0.1', 1042))
    print(s.recv(4096))  # for the hello message

    s.send(b'{"type":"request-file-analysis","content":"x <- 1","id":"1"}\n')

    print(s.recv(65536))  # for the response (please use a more sophisticated mechanism)
```


</details>
</li>

</ol>
